[preface]
== Versions


This specification documents the following extension versions:

* Xqci@0.13.0
* Xqcia@0.7.0
* Xqciac@0.3.0
* Xqcibi@0.2.0
* Xqcibm@0.8.0
* Xqcicli@0.3.0
* Xqcicm@0.2.0
* Xqcics@0.2.0
* Xqcicsr@0.4.0
* Xqciint@0.10.0
* Xqciio@0.1.0
* Xqcilb@0.2.0
* Xqcili@0.2.0
* Xqcilia@0.2.0
* Xqcilo@0.3.0
* Xqcilsm@0.6.0
* Xqcisim@0.2.0
* Xqcisls@0.2.0
* Xqcisync@0.3.0


=== Version History

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
|===
2+^| Xqci

h| 0.13.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! nonstandard-released
h! Changes a!

    * Fix version history of releases v0.11.0 and v0.12.0
    * Fix description and IDL code of qc.csrrwr instruction to allow just read CSR
    * Fix IDL code of qc.c.mileaveret instruction to avoid restoring from stack NMIP and EXCP bits


!===
h| 0.12.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix desciption of qc.c.eir instruction to match IDL code and functionality
    * Fix encoding of qc.swm and qc.swmi instructions to state that rs3 cannot be x0
    * Fix description and IDL code of qc.swm and qc.lwm instructions to state that length is in rs2[4:0]


!===
h| 0.11.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix IDL code of qc.shlusat instruction (should use zero-extension and not sign-extension)
    * Fix IDL code of qc.shlusat and qc.shlsat instructions (should compare values of xlen()*2 bits)
    * Fix IDL code of qc.shlusat and qc.shlsat instructions because change in IDL operators (width adjustment)
    * Fix IDL code of qc.subsat, qc.addusat and qc.addsat instructions because change in IDL operators (width adjustment)
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.mileaveret, qc.c.mnret and qc.c.mret instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.clrint, qc.c.setint, qc.clrinti and qc.setinti instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.di, qc.c.dir, qc.c.ei, qc.c.eir and qc.c.mienter.nest instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.sync, qc.c.syncr, qc.c.syncwf and qc.c.syncwl instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.bseti, qc.c.extu, qc.ext and qc.extu instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.extd, qc.extdu, qc.extdr and qc.extdur instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.extdpr, qc.extdprh, qc.extdupr and qc.extduprh instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.insb, qc.insbi, qc.insbr and qc.insbri instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator
    * Fix IDL code for qc.insbh, qc.insbhr, qc.insbpr and qc.insbprh instructions because change in IDL '<<' operator


!===
h| 0.10.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix IDL code for Smdbltrp and Smrnmi spec compatibility for qc.c.mileaveret instruction


!===
h| 0.9.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix IDL code sign extension logic for qc.e.lb and qc.e.lh instructions
    * Fix IDL code sign extension logic for qc.ext and qc.extd instructions
    * Fix IDL code sign extension logic for qc.extdpr, qc.extdprh and qc.extdr instructions
    * Fix IDL code and description increasing shift to 6 bit for qc.extdr and qc.extdur instructions
    * Fix IDL code and description increasing shift to 6 bit for qc.extdpr and qc.extdprh instructions
    * Fix IDL code and description increasing shift to 6 bit for qc.extdupr and qc.extduprh instructions
    * Fix IDL code sign extension logic for qc.lieq instruction
    * Fix wrong mantissa bit selection in qc.norm, qc.normu and qc.normeu instructions
    * Fix wrong exponent calculation in qc.normeu instruction
    * Fix IDL code and description of qc.setwm instruction to state that number of words written 0..31.
    * Fix IDL code for Smdbltrp and Smrnmi spec compatibility for qc.c.mret and qc.c.mnret instructions


!===
h| 0.8.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix rs1 cannot be 31 for qc.extdu, qc.extd, qc.extdur, instructions
    * Fix rs1 cannot be 31 for qc.extduprh, qc.extdprh, qc.extdupr, qc.extdr qc.extdpr instructions
    * Fix typos in IDL code (missing ')' ) for qc.extdpr, qc.extdr instructions
    * Fix IDL code and description to look correct in PDF for qc.insbhr and qc.insbh instructions
    * Fix Xqci extension description to reflect correct 48-bit format field names
    * Fix IDL code to to match description for qc.insbr instruction
    * Add stack checks to qc.c.mienter, qc.c.mienter.nest, qc.c.mileaveret


!===
h| 0.7.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix typos in description of qc.shlsat and qc.shlusat instructions
    * Fix bug in qc.shlsat that caused wrong IDL code result
    * Fix clobbering of saturation results in [add/addu/sub]sat instructions
    * Rename all custom CSRs of the Xqciint extension to use dot as separator in the name
    * Fix addresses of qc.mclicie* CSRs to 0x7f8-0x7ff (was copy & paste from qc.mclicip*)
    * Add missing CSR registers qc.mclicilvl00 - qc.mclicilvl31
    * Add missing CSR registers qc.mwpstartaddr0 - qc.mwpstartaddr3 and qc.mwpendaddr0 - qc.mwpendaddr3
    * Add missing CSR registers qc.mstkbottomaddr and qc.mstktopaddr
    * Add missing CSR registers qc.mmcr, qc.mthreadptr, qc.mcause
    * Remove CSR registers qc.mncause, qc.mnepc
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.mienter, qc.c.mienter.nest, qc.c.mileaveret, qc.c.mret, qc.c.mnret
    * Fix IDL code for qc.c.ei, qc.c.eir, qc.c.di, qc.c.dir
    * Add list of supported custom exceptions
    * Fix qc.cto instruction IDL code
    * Change width calculations for qc.extdpr, qc.extdprh, qc.extdr, qc.extdupr, qc.extduprh, qc.extdur,
    * Change width calculations for qc.insbhr, qc.insbpr, qc.insbprh, qc.insbr, qc.insbri


!===
h| 0.6.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Fix encoding of qc.c.extu instruction
    * Fix encoding of qc.swmi instruction
    * Fix decoding of qc.pputci instruction
    * Fix decoding of qc.c.delay instruction (state that immediate cannot be 0)
    * Rename qc.slasat -> qc.shlsat
    * Rename qc.sllsat -> qc.shlusat
    * Add requirement to include Zca extension for Xqcisim since it has 16-bit instructions
    * Add requirement to include Zca extension for Xqcisync since it has 16-bit instructions
    * Remove qc.flags CSR


!===
h| 0.5.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Added Xqciio sub-extension
    * Added Xqcisim sub-extension
    * Added Xqcisync sub-extension
    * Rename instruction of qc.muladdi to qc.muliadd
    * Rename instruction of qc.c.muladdi to qc.c.muliadd
    * Fix description of qc.shladd instruction
    * Fix description and functionality of qc.c.extu instruction
    * Fix description and functionality of qc.wrapi instruction
    * Fix description of qc.swmi, qc.lwmi and qc.setwmi instructions
    * Fix description of qc.mclici* CSRs to reflect being part of Xqciint custom extension
    * Fix description of qc.setinti and qc.clrinti instructions
    * Fix to make qc.c.mret and qc.c.mnret visible


!===
h| 0.4.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! frozen
h! Changes a!

    * Add information about instruction formats of each instruction
    * Fix description and functionality of qc.c.extu instruction
    * Fix description and functionality of qc.shladd instruction


!===
h| 0.3.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! development
h! Changes a!

    * Rename extension and sub extensions to match toolchain guidelines
    * Rename mnemonics to match toolchain guidelines
    * Ensure every instruction belongs to at least one sub extension


!===
h| 0.2.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

h! State ! development
h! Changes a!

    * Splits Xqci into sub-extensions based on instruction type
    * Removed shXadd instructions in favor of generic shladd


!===
h| 0.1.0
a|

[frame="none",grid="none",cols="1,4"]
!===

<<<
== Conventions

Version requirements are specified as conditions using the following operators:

[cols="1,2"]
|===
| Operator | Meaning

| `~> VERSION` | Accepts any version that is _compatible_ with `VERSION`. By default, a version A is compatible with a version B if A's version number is greater than or equal to version B. If that default assumption is ever broken, it will be noted in the list of extension versions.
| `= VERSION` | Accepts only version `VERSION`.
| `>= VERSION` | Accepts any version greater than or equal to `VERSION`.
| `\<= VERSION` | Accepts any version less than or equal to `VERSION`.
| `> VERSION` | Accepts any version greater than `VERSION`.
| `< VERSION` | Accepts any version less than `VERSION`.
|===

<<<
== Extension description


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqci extension includes a set of instructions that improve RISC-V code density and
performance in microcontrollers. It fills several gaps:

Long immediates::
--
This extension provides wide-immediate versions of
loads, stores, branches, jumps, and several arithmetic operations.
--

Addressing modes::
--
New indexed addressing modes are added for load and store instructions.
--

Load/store multiple::
--
Xqci adds instructions that load multiple sequential values from memory into multiple registers.
Analogous instructions for stores are also included.
--

Branch immediate instructions::
--
The base RISC-V ISA provides conditional branches that compare two register values.
Xqci adds conditional branch instructions that compare an immediate value to a register value,
reducing a common code sequence into a single instruction.
--

Conditional instructions::
--
Xqci includes a variety of conditional select instructions that pick one of two operand values based on the result of a condition
and conditional move instructions that either move a value or retain a value in a destination register based on the result of a condition.
Conditional select and conditional move instructions help reduce code size and avoid branches in common code sequences.
--

Extra bit manipulation instructions::
--
Xqci expands upon the standard xref:#udb-extension-B[`B`] extension by adding instructions for
bit insertion/extraction, bit set/clear, sign and zero extension, and bit counting instructions.
--

Fast interrupt instructions::
--
Xqci adds instructions to accelerate interrupt handling, including instructions to quickly
enable/disable interrupts and instructions to automatically save an interrupt frame.
--

Saturating arithmetic::
--
Xqci adds saturating arithmetic instructions to improve performance of fixed-point calculations.
--

Xqci adds 16, 32, and 48-bit instruction encodings. The 16 and 32-bit encodings are allocated
in the custom opcode space so as not to conflict with standard RISC-V instructions. The 48-bit instructions
follow the guidance for 48-bit instructions in the RISC-V standard, but are not allocated in reserved custom
space since no such space has been defined by RISC-V International.

Extension-specific instruction formats ::
--
QC.EAI format used for 48-bit instructions that operate on 32-bit immediate argument.
--

[%autowidth, cols="4*", options="header" ]
|===
^|Field
^|Start bit
^|Width
^|Description

|opcode
^|0
^|7
|Opcode field of 48-bit instructions is 0x1F

|rd
^|7
^|5
|Destination register

|funct3
^|12
^|3
|Function field identifying instruction group

|f1
^|15
^|1
|Secondary function field

|imm[31:0]
^|16
^|32
|Immediate operand of 32 bits
|===

--
QC.EI format used for 48-bit instructions that operate on 26-bit immediate argument, including loads.
--

[%autowidth, cols="4*", options="header" ]
|===
^|Field
^|Start bit
^|Width
^|Description

|opcode
^|0
^|7
|Opcode field of 48-bit instructions is 0x1F

|rd
^|7
^|5
|Destination register

|funct3
^|12
^|3
|Function field identifying instruction group

|rs1
^|15
^|5
|Register argument

|imm[9:0]
^|20
^|10
|Immediate operand of 26 bits, the 10 LSBs

|funct2
^|30
^|2
|Secondary function field

|imm[25:10]
^|32
^|16
|Immediate operand of 26 bits, the 16 MSBs
|===

--
QC.EB format used for 48-bit branch instructions that compare register with 16-bit immediate.
--

[%autowidth, cols="4*", options="header" ]
|===
^|Field
^|Start bit
^|Width
^|Description

|opcode
^|0
^|7
|Opcode field of 48-bit instructions is 0x1F

|imm[4:1,11]
^|7
^|5
|Bits of immediate value of branch target

|funct3
^|12
^|3
|Function field identifying instruction group

|rs1
^|15
^|5
|Register argument

|funct5
^|20
^|5
|Secondary function field

|imm[12,10:5]
^|25
^|7
|Bits of immediate value of branch target

|simm[15:0]
^|32
^|16
|Immediate operand of 16 bits to compare with register
|===

--
QC.EJ format used for 48-bit jump/call instructions with 32-bit immediate target address.
--

[%autowidth, cols="4*", options="header" ]
|===
^|Field
^|Start bit
^|Width
^|Description

|opcode
^|0
^|7
|Opcode field of 48-bit instructions is 0x1F

|imm[4:1,11]
^|7
^|5
|Bits of immediate value of branch target

|funct3
^|12
^|3
|Function field identifying instruction group

|funct2
^|15
^|2
|Secondary function field

|imm[15:13]
^|17
^|3
|Bits of immediate value of branch target

|funct5
^|20
^|5
|Secondary function field

|imm[12,10:5]
^|25
^|7
|Bits of immediate value of branch target

|imm[31:16]
^|32
^|16
|The 16 MSBs of immediate value of branch target
|===

--
QC.ES format used for 48-bit store instructions with 26-bit immediate offset.
--

[%autowidth.stretch]
|===
|Field|Start bit|Width|Description

|opcode
^|0
^|7
|Opcode field of 48-bit instructions is 0x1F

|imm[4:0]
^|7
^|5
|Immediate operand of 26 bits offset, the 5 LSBs

|funct3
^|12
^|3
|Function field identifying instruction group

|rs1
^|15
^|5
|Register argument used as base address

|rs2
^|20
^|5
|Register argument to be saved

|imm[9:5]
^|25
^|5
|Immediate operand of 26 bits offset, the 5 bits

|funct2
^|30
^|2
|Secondary function field

|imm[25:10]
^|32
^|16
|Immediate operand of 26 bits offset, the 16 MSBs
|===

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcia extension includes eleven instructions to perform integer arithmetic.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqciac extension includes three instructions to accelerate common
address calculations.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcibi extension includes twelve conditional branch instructions that use an immediate
operand for a source.

All instructions in Xqcibi following the same relocation type as standard RISC-V branches
in the base architecture (e.g., BEQ, BNE, etc.).

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcibm extension includes thirty eight instructions that perform bit manipulation,
include insertion and extraction.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcicli extension includes twelve instructions that conditionally
load an immediate value.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcicm extension includes thirteen conditional move instructions.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcics extension includes eight conditional select instructions.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcicsr extension contains two instructions to read/write CSR which index is in register and not immediate.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqciint extension includes eleven instructions to accelerate interrupt
servicing by performing common actions during ISR prologue/epilogue.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqciio extension includes two instructions to access external non-memory-mapped devices for input and output

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcilb extension includes two 48-bit instructions to encode a long branch.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcili extension includes a two instructions that load large immediates than is available
with the base RISC-V ISA.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcilia extension includes eight 48-bit instructions that perform arithmetic using
large immediates.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcilo extension includes eight 48-bit load/stores instructions that use an offset
larger than can be found in the base RISC-V ISA.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcilsm extension includes six instructions that transfer multiple values
between registers and memory.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcisim extension includes ten hint instructions to interface simulation environment.
On real target any instruction from this extension executed as "no-operation" and have no effect.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcisls extension includes five load and three store instructions with a scaled index addressing mode.

:leveloffset: -2


:leveloffset: +2
The Xqcisync extension includes nine instructions, eight for non-memory-mapped devices synchronization and delay instruction.
Synchronization instructions are kind of IO fences that work with special devices synchronization signals.

:leveloffset: -2








<<<
== Instruction list

=== Xqci




The following 157 instructions are implied by the requirements
of this extension.

.Xqci = 0.13.0 requirements
--
++(++++(++xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciac[`Xqciac`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibm[`Xqcibm`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcicli[`Xqcicli`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcicm[`Xqcicm`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcicsr[`Xqcicsr`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciio[`Xqciio`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilb[`Xqcilb`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcili[`Xqcili`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilia[`Xqcilia`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilo[`Xqcilo`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilsm[`Xqcilsm`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisls[`Xqcisls`] && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisync[`Xqcisync`]) && !`D`)
--

.Instructions implied by Xqci = 0.13.0
[cols="4,4,1",separator="^"]
|===
^ Mnemonic ^ Instruction ^ Defined by

^ `qc.addsat rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_addsat[Saturating signed addition]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.addusat rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_addusat[Saturating unsigned addition]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.beqi rs1, imm, offset`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_beqi[Branch on equal (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`])
^ `qc.bgei rs1, imm, offset`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_bgei[Branch on greater than or equal (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`])
^ `qc.bgeui rs1, imm, offset`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_bgeui[Branch on greater than or equal unsigned (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`])
^ `qc.blti rs1, imm, offset`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_blti[Branch on less than (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`])
^ `qc.bltui rs1, imm, offset`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_bltui[Branch on less than unsigned (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`])
^ `qc.bnei rs1, imm, offset`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_bnei[Branch on not equal (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibi[`Xqcibi`])
^ `qc.brev32 rd, rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_brev32[Reverse bit order]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibm[`Xqcibm`])
^ `qc.c.bexti rd, shamt`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_bexti[Single-Bit extract (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibm[`Xqcibm`])
^ `qc.c.bseti rd, shamt`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_bseti[Single-Bit set (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibm[`Xqcibm`])
^ `qc.c.clrint rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_clrint[Clear interrupt (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ `qc.c.delay imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_delay[Delay execution for immediate amount of cycles]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisync[`Xqcisync`])
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_di[`qc.c.di`]
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_di[Disable interrupts]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ `qc.c.dir rd`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_dir[Disable interrupts (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_ei[`qc.c.ei`]
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_ei[Enable interrupts]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ `qc.c.eir rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_eir[Restore interrupts (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ `qc.c.extu rd, width`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_extu[Extract bits unsigned]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcibm[`Xqcibm`])
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_mienter[`qc.c.mienter`]
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_mienter[Machine mode interrupt enter]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_mienter_nest[`qc.c.mienter.nest`]
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_mienter_nest[Machine mode interrupt enter]

a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.pexit rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_pexit[Exit call with register argument pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.ppreg rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_ppreg[Print register pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_ppregs[`qc.ppregs`]
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_ppregs[Print all registers pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.pputc rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_pputc[Print character passed in register argument pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.pputci imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_pputci[Print character passed in the immediate argument pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.pputs rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_pputs[Print string pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.psyscall rs1`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_psyscall[System call with register argument pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.psyscalli imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_psyscalli[System call with immediate argument pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisim[`Xqcisim`])
^ `qc.selecteqi rd, imm, rs2, rs3`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selecteqi[Select load immediate or register if equal (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectieq rd, rs1, rs2, simm2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectieq[Select load immediate or register if equal (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectieqi rd, imm, rs2, simm2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectieqi[Select load immediate or register if equal (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectiieq rd, rs1, simm1, simm2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectiieq[Select load immediate if equal (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectiine rd, rs1, simm1, simm2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectiine[Select load immediate if not equal (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectine rd, rs1, rs2, simm2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectine[Select load immediate or register if not equal (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectinei rd, imm, rs2, simm2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectinei[Select load immediate or register if not equal (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.selectnei rd, imm, rs2, rs3`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_selectnei[Select load immediate or register if not equal (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcics[`Xqcics`])
^ `qc.setinti imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_setinti[Set interrupt (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
^ `qc.setwm rs3, rs2, imm(rs1)`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_setwm[Set word multiple (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilsm[`Xqcilsm`])
^ `qc.setwmi rs3, length, imm(rs1)`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_setwmi[Set word multiple (Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilsm[`Xqcilsm`])
^ `qc.shladd rd, rs1, rs2, shamt`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_shladd[Shift left and add (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && ++(++xref:#udb-extension-Xqci[`Xqci`] pass:[||] xref:#udb-extension-Xqciac[`Xqciac`]))
^ `qc.shlsat rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_shlsat[Saturating signed left shift]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.shlusat rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_shlusat[Saturating unsigned left shift]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.srb rs3, rs1, rs2, shamt`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_srb[Store indexed byte]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisls[`Xqcisls`])
^ `qc.srh rs3, rs1, rs2, shamt`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_srh[Store indexed halfword]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisls[`Xqcisls`])
^ `qc.srw rs3, rs1, rs2, shamt`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_srw[Store indexed word]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisls[`Xqcisls`])
^ `qc.subsat rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_subsat[Saturating signed subtraction]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.subusat rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_subusat[Saturating unsigned subtraction]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.swm rs3, rs2, imm(rs1)`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_swm[Store word multiple]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilsm[`Xqcilsm`])
^ `qc.swmi rs3, length, imm(rs1)`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_swmi[Store word multiple (immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcilsm[`Xqcilsm`])
^ `qc.sync imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_sync[Non-memory-mapped device read-after-write synchronization to completion]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisync[`Xqcisync`])
^ `qc.syncr imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_syncr[Non-memory-mapped device read-after-write synchronization]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisync[`Xqcisync`])
^ `qc.syncwf imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_syncwf[Non-memory-mapped device write-after-read synchronization]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisync[`Xqcisync`])
^ `qc.syncwl imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_syncwl[Non-memory-mapped device write-after-read synchronization to completion]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcisync[`Xqcisync`])
^ `qc.wrap rd, rs1, rs2`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_wrap[Wraparound (Register)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])
^ `qc.wrapi rd, rs1, imm`
^ xref:#udb-insn-qc_wrapi[Wraparound (Unsigned Immediate)]
a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqcia[`Xqcia`])

=== Xqciio


The following 2 instructions must be implemented when Xqciio is implemented:

.Instructions defined by Xqciio = 0.1.0
[cols="1,1,5,5"]
|===
| RV32 | RV64 | Mnemonic | Instruction 
| &#x2713;
| 
| `qc.inw rd, imm(rs1)`
| xref:#udb-insn-qc_inw[Input word from non-memory-mapped device]
| &#x2713;
| 
| `qc.outw rs2, imm(rs1)`
| xref:#udb-insn-qc_outw[Output word to non-memory-mapped device]
|===

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mcause]
= qc.mcause

*Machine Mode Custom Cause Register*

Machine Mode Custom Cause Register / Interrupt context register.


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && ++(++xref:#udb-extension-Xqci[`Xqci`] pass:[||] xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`]))
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqci ! Qualcomm uC extensions

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7c9
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mcause format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":12,"name":"EXCCODE","type":3},{"bits":4,"name":"MIL","type":3},{"bits":4,"name":"MPIL","type":3},{"bits":4,"name":"MNPIL","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"NMIP","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"EXCP","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"MIE","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"MPIE","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"MNPIE","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"MPDT","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"NMIE","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"INT","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}
....

== Fields


[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:INT]
=== `INT`

[example]
--
Location::
31

Description::
Alias of mcause.INT bit, if 1'b1 - interrupt processing, if 1'b0 - exception processing.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:NMIE]
=== `NMIE`

[example]
--
Location::
30

Description::
Alias of mnstatus.NMIE, if 1'b0, currently processing NMI or double trap.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MPDT]
=== `MPDT`

[example]
--
Location::
29

Description::
M-mode Previous Disable Trap, value of mstatush.MDT at the moment of interrupt/exception.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MNPIE]
=== `MNPIE`

[example]
--
Location::
28

Description::
M-mode NMI Previous Interrupt Enable, value of mstatus.MIE at the moment of NMI/double trap.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MPIE]
=== `MPIE`

[example]
--
Location::
27

Description::
Alias of mstatus.MPIE, M-mode Previous Interrupt Enable.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MIE]
=== `MIE`

[example]
--
Location::
26

Description::
Alias of mstatus.MIE, M-mode Interrupt Enable.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:EXCP]
=== `EXCP`

[example]
--
Location::
25

Description::
Exception Pending Bit, cleaned when exception acknowledged.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:NMIP]
=== `NMIP`

[example]
--
Location::
24

Description::
NMI Pending Bit, cleaned when NMI acknowledged.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MNPIL]
=== `MNPIL`

[example]
--
Location::
23:20

Description::
M-mode NMI Previous Interrupt Level, value of qc.mcause.MIL at the moment of NMI/double trap.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MPIL]
=== `MPIL`

[example]
--
Location::
19:16

Description::
M-mode Previous Interrupt Level, value of qc.mcause.MIL at the moment of interrupt/exception.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:MIL]
=== `MIL`

[example]
--
Location::
15:12

Description::
M-mode Interrupt Level.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
15

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mcause:EXCCODE]
=== `EXCCODE`

[example]
--
Location::
11:0

Description::
Alias of mcause.EXCCODE[11:0], Interrupt/Exception code ID.

Type::
RW-H

Reset value::
0

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicie0]
= qc.mclicie0

*IRQ Enable 0*

Enable bits for IRQs 0-31


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7f8
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicie1]
= qc.mclicie1

*IRQ Enable 1*

Enable bits for IRQs 32-63


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7f9
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicie1 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ32","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ33","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ34","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ35","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ36","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ37","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ38","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ39","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ40","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ41","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ42","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ43","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ44","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ45","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ46","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ47","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ48","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ49","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ50","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ51","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ52","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ53","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ54","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ55","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ56","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ57","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ58","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ59","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ60","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ61","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ62","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ63","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicie2]
= qc.mclicie2

*IRQ Enable 2*

Enable bits for IRQs 64-95


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])

a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7fa
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M

== Format
.qc.mclicie2 format

:leveloffset: -2

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicie3]
= qc.mclicie3

*IRQ Enable 3*

Enable bits for IRQs 96-127


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7fb
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicie3 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ96","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ97","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ98","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ99","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ100","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ101","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ102","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ103","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ104","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ105","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ106","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ107","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ108","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ109","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ110","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ111","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ112","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ113","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ114","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ115","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ116","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ117","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ118","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ119","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ120","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ121","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ122","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ123","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ124","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ125","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ126","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ127","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}
....

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicie4]
= qc.mclicie4

*IRQ Enable 4*

Enable bits for IRQs 128-159


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7fc
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicie4 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ128","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ129","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ130","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ131","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ132","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ133","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ134","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ135","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ136","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ137","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ138","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ139","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ140","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ141","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ142","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ143","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ144","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ145","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ146","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ147","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ148","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ149","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ150","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ151","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ152","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ153","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ154","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ155","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ156","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ157","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ158","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ159","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicie6]
= qc.mclicie6

*IRQ Enable 6*

Enable bits for IRQs 192-223


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7fe
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicie6 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ192","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ193","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ194","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ195","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ196","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ197","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ198","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ199","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ200","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ201","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ202","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ203","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ204","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ205","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ206","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ207","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ208","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ209","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ210","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ211","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ212","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ213","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ214","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ215","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ216","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ217","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ218","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ219","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ220","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ221","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ222","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ223","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}

*IRQ Level 0*

Level bits for IRQs 0-7


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0xbc0
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

= qc.mclicilvl15

*IRQ Level 15*

Level bits for IRQs 120-127


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0xbcf
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicilvl15 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicip0]
= qc.mclicip0

*IRQ Pending 0*

Pending bits for IRQs 0-31


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

= qc.mclicip1

*IRQ Pending 1*

Pending bits for IRQs 32-63


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===

!===

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicip2]
= qc.mclicip2

*IRQ Pending 2*

Pending bits for IRQs 64-95


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7f2
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicip2 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ64","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ65","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ66","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ67","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ68","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ69","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ70","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ71","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ72","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ73","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ74","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ75","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ76","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ77","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ78","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ79","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ80","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ81","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ82","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ83","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ84","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ85","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ86","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ87","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ88","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ89","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ90","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ91","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ92","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ93","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ94","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ95","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicip4]
= qc.mclicip4

*IRQ Pending 4*

Pending bits for IRQs 128-159


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7f4
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicip4 format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ128","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ129","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ130","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ131","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ132","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ133","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ134","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ135","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ136","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ137","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ138","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ139","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ140","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ141","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ142","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ143","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ144","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ145","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ146","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ147","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ148","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ149","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ150","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ151","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ152","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ153","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ154","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ155","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ156","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ157","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ158","type":3},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQ159","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}

= qc.mclicip5

== Attributes

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mclicip6]
= qc.mclicip6

*IRQ Pending 6*

Pending bits for IRQs 192-223


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7f6
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicip6 format

= qc.mclicip7

*IRQ Pending 7*

Pending bits for IRQs 224-255


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])

a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7f7
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mclicip7 format

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mmcr]
= qc.mmcr

*Machine Mode Control Register*

Machine Mode Control Register.


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7c0
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mmcr format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":4,"name":"WP_EXEC","type":3},{"bits":4,"name":"WP_WRITE","type":3},{"bits":4,"name":"WP_READ","type":3},{"bits":9,"type":1},{"bits":1,"name":"IRQNE","type":3},{"bits":10,"type":1}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}
....

== Field Summary

[%autowidth,separator=@,float="center",align="center",cols="^,<,<,<",options="header",role="stretch"]
|===
@Name @ Location @ Type @ Reset Value

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mmcr-WP_EXEC[qc.mmcr.WP_EXEC]
@ 3:0
@ RW
@ 0

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mmcr-WP_WRITE[qc.mmcr.WP_WRITE]
@ 7:4
@ RW
@ 0

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mmcr-WP_READ[qc.mmcr.WP_READ]
@ 11:8
@ RW
@ 0

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mmcr-IRQNE[qc.mmcr.IRQNE]
@ 21
@ RW
@ 0

|===


== Fields


[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mmcr:WP_EXEC]
=== `WP_EXEC`

[example]
--
Location::
3:0

Description::
Watchpoint execution enable (WP 0-3)

Type::
RW

Reset value::
0

--

=== `WP_WRITE`

[example]
--

7:4

Description::

Type::
RW

Reset value::
0

[example]

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mntvec]
= qc.mntvec

*Machine Non-Maskable Interrupt Vector Control*

Controls where NMI jump.

== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7c3
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mntvec format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":2,"type":1},{"bits":30,"name":"BASE","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}
....

== Field Summary

[%autowidth,separator=@,float="center",align="center",cols="^,<,<,<",options="header",role="stretch"]
|===
@Name @ Location @ Type @ Reset Value

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mntvec-BASE[qc.mntvec.BASE]
@ 31:2
@ RW-R
@ 0

|===


== Fields


[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mntvec:BASE]
=== `BASE`

[example]
--
Location::
31:2

Description::
Bits [MXLEN-1:2] of the NMI vector physical address for any NMI taken in M-mode.


Type::
RW-R

Reset value::
0

--


== Software write

This CSR may store a value that is different from what software attempts to write.

When a software write occurs (_e.g._, through xref:#udb-insn-csrrw[`csrrw`]), the following determines the
written value:

[source,idl]
----
BASE = return csr_value.BASE;

----


:leveloffset: -2
<<<
:leveloffset: +2

[#udb:doc:csr:qc_mstkbottomaddr]
= qc.mstkbottomaddr

*Machine Stack Bottom Limit*

Stack bottom limit register. If the stack pointer (sp == x2) lesser then its value - SpOutOfRange exception occurs


== Attributes
[%autowidth,separator="^"]
|===
h^ Requirement a^ ++(++xlen+++()+++ == 32 && xref:#udb-extension-Xqciint[`Xqciint`])
h^ Defining extensions
a^

!===

h! Xqciint ! Qualcomm interrupt prologue/epilogue
!===

h^ CSR Address    ^ 0x7c5
h^ Length         ^ 32-bit
h^ Privilege Mode ^ M
|===

== Format
.qc.mstkbottomaddr format
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":4,"name":"RESERVED","type":3},{"bits":28,"name":"STKADDR","type":3}],"config":{"bits":32,"lanes":2}}
....

== Field Summary

[%autowidth,separator=@,float="center",align="center",cols="^,<,<,<",options="header",role="stretch"]
|===
@Name @ Location @ Type @ Reset Value

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mstkbottomaddr-STKADDR[qc.mstkbottomaddr.STKADDR]
@ 31:4
@ RW
@ 0

@ xref:#udb-csrfield-qc_mstkbottomaddr-RESERVED[qc.mstkbottomaddr.RESERVED]
@ 3:0
@ RO
@ 0

|===


== Fields


[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mstkbottomaddr:STKADDR]
=== `STKADDR`

[example]
--
Location::
31:4

Description::
If the stack pointer (sp == x2) lesser then STKADDR*16 - SpOutOfRange exception occurs


Type::
RW

Reset value::
0

--

[#udb:doc:csr_field:qc_mstkbottomaddr:RESERVED]
=== `RESERVED`

[example]
--
Location::
3:0

Description::
Reserved and must be zero

Type::
RO

Reset value::
0

--

== Instructions (in alphabetical order)

:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_addsat]
= qc.addsat

Synopsis::
Saturating signed addition

Mnemonic::
----
qc.addsat rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xe,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Add signed values `rs1` and `rs2`, saturate the signed result, and write to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> sum = X[rs1] pass:[`]pass:[+] X[rs2];
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> most_negative_number = {2'b11, {(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1){1'b0}}};
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> most_positive_number = {2'b00, {(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1){1'b1}}};
if pass:[(]X[rs1][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1] == X[rs2][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1]) {
  if pass:[(]sum[xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1] != X[rs1][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1]) {
    if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++X[rs1]) < 's0) {
      sum = most_negative_number;
    } else {
      sum = most_positive_number;
    }
  }
}
X[rd] = sum[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_addsat[`qc.addsat`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_addusat]
= qc.addusat

Synopsis::
Saturating unsigned addition

Mnemonic::
----
qc.addusat rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xf,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Add unsigned values `rs1` and `rs2`, saturate the unsigned result, and write to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> sum = X[rs1] pass:[`]pass:[+] X[rs2];
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> largest_unsigned_value = {1'b0, {xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]){1'b1}}};
if pass:[(]sum > largest_unsigned_value) {
  X[rd] = largest_unsigned_value[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
} else {
  X[rd] = sum[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_addusat[`qc.addusat`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_beqi]
= qc.beqi

Synopsis::
Branch on equal (Immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.beqi rs1, imm, offset
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x7b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "offset[4:1|11]","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "imm != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": "offset[12|10:5]","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Branches to `PC` + `offset` if the value in `rs1` is equal to the signed immediate
Instruction encoded in BI instruction format



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
signed Bits<13> offset = sext({$encoding[31], $encoding[7], $encoding[30:25], $encoding[11:8], 1'd0}, 13);
Bits<5> imm = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++X[rs1]) == $signed+++(+++imm)) {
  xref:#udb-function-jump_halfword[jump_halfword]pass:[(]$pc pass:[+] $signed+++(+++offset));
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_beqi[`qc.beqi`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0



| *Xqcibi*
| = 0.2.0
















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

  xref:#udb-function-jump_halfword[jump_halfword]pass:[(]$pc pass:[+] $signed+++(+++offset));

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_brev32]
= qc.brev32

Synopsis::

Mnemonic::
----
qc.brev32 rd, rs1
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0xc0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Reverses the bit order of `rs1` and writes the result to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg orig_val = X[rs1];
XReg tmp;
for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]); i++) {
  tmp[xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1 - i] = orig_val[i];
}
X[rd] = tmp;
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_brev32[`qc.brev32`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_bexti]
= qc.c.bexti

Synopsis::
Single-Bit extract (Immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.bexti rd, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":2,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "shamt != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":6,"name": 0x24,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
This instruction returns a single bit extracted from `rd`.
The index is read from the lower log2(XLEN) bits of `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in CB instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> shamt = $encoding[6:2];
Bits<3> rd = $encoding[9:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg index = shamt & (xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1);
XReg reg = xref:#udb-function-creg2reg[creg2reg]pass:[(]rd);
X[reg] = (X[reg] >> index) & 1;
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_bexti[`qc.c.bexti`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_bseti]
= qc.c.bseti

Synopsis::
Single-Bit set (Immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.bseti rd, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":2,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "shamt != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":6,"name": 0x25,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
This instruction returns `rd` with a single bit set at the index specified in shamt.
The index is read from the lower log2(XLEN) bits of `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in CB instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> shamt = $encoding[6:2];
Bits<3> rd = $encoding[9:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg index = shamt & (xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1);
XReg reg = xref:#udb-function-creg2reg[creg2reg]pass:[(]rd);
X[reg] = X[reg] | (MXLEN'b1 << index);
----


Included in::

| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*

| *Xqcibm*

XReg pre_qc_mcause_masked = pre_qc_mcause & ~(32'b1 << 26);

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_extu]
= qc.c.extu

Synopsis::
Extract bits unsigned

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.extu rd, width
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":2,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "width_minus1 != {0,1,2,3,4}","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":4,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Extract a subset of bits from `rd` starting from LSB.
The width of the subset is determined by (`width_minus1`[4:0] + 1) (1..32).
Instruction encoded in CI instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> width_minus1 = $encoding[6:2];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg width = width_minus1 pass:[+] 1;
X[rd] = (X[rd] >> 0) & ((32'b1 << width) - 1);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_extu[`qc.c.extu`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

----

Encoding::

....
{"reg":[{"bits":16,"name": 0x1812,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Machine mode interrupt enter, interrupt nesting is disabled.
Interrupt frame is saved in the stack.
Interrupts are disabled.
Instruction encoded in CI instruction format.



Decode Variables::


qc.c.mienter has no decode variables.



Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

XReg mepc_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mepc[CSR[mepc]]].sw_read();
XReg mnepc_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnepc[CSR[mnepc]]].sw_read();
XReg qc_mcause_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mcause[CSR[qc.mcause]]].sw_read();
XReg reserved_val = 0;
if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-NMIE[NMIE] == 1'b1) {
  xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 4, mepc_val, $encoding);
} else {
  xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 4, mnepc_val, $encoding);
}
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 8, X[8][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 12, qc_mcause_val, $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 16, X[1][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 20, reserved_val, $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 24, X[5][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 28, X[6][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 32, X[7][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 36, X[10][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 40, X[11][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 44, X[12][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 48, X[13][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 52, X[14][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 56, X[15][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 60, X[16][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 64, X[17][31:0], $encoding);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 68, X[28][31:0], $encoding);

XReg virtual_address = virtual_address_sp pass:[+] 96;
XReg prev_retpc = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 4, $encoding);
XReg qc_mcause_val = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 12, $encoding);
Bits<1> nmie_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-NMIE[NMIE];
XReg qc_mcause_prev_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mcause[CSR[qc.mcause]]].sw_read();
XReg qc_mcause_nmip_excp_mask = (32'b1 << 24) | (32'b1 << 25);
XReg qc_mcause_new_val = (qc_mcause_val & ~qc_mcause_nmip_excp_mask) | (qc_mcause_prev_val & qc_mcause_nmip_excp_mask);
CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mcause[CSR[qc.mcause]]].sw_write(qc_mcause_new_val);
X[8] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 8, $encoding);
X[1] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 16, $encoding);
X[5] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 24, $encoding);
X[6] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 28, $encoding);
X[7] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 32, $encoding);
X[10] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 36, $encoding);
X[11] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 40, $encoding);
X[12] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 44, $encoding);
X[13] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 48, $encoding);
X[14] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 52, $encoding);
X[15] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 56, $encoding);
X[16] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 60, $encoding);
X[17] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 64, $encoding);
X[28] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 68, $encoding);
X[29] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 72, $encoding);
X[30] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 76, $encoding);
X[31] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, virtual_address - 80, $encoding);
X[2] = X[2] pass:[+] 96;
if pass:[(]nmie_val == 1'b1) {
  XReg qc_mcause_val_masked = qc_mcause_new_val & ~(32'b1 << 26) & ~(32'b1 << 27) & ~(32'b1 << 29) & ~(32'hFF << 12);
  Bits<1> mpie_val = (qc_mcause_val >> 27) & 1;
  Bits<1> mpdt_val = (qc_mcause_val >> 29) & 1;
  Bits<4> mpil_val = (qc_mcause_val >> 16) & 0xF;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MIE[MIE] = mpie_val;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPIE[MPIE] = 1'b1;
  if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Smdbltrp)) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatush[mstatush]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatush-MDT[MDT] = mpdt_val;
  }
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mcause[CSR[qc.mcause]]].sw_write(qc_mcause_val_masked | (32'b1 << 27) | (mpie_val pass:[`]<< 26) | (32'b0 << 29) | (mpil_val pass:[`]<< 12) | (32'b1111 << 16));
  if pass:[(]mpdt_val == 1'b0) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] != 2'b11) {
      CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPRV[MPRV] = 0;
    }
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] == 2'b00) {
      xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]PrivilegeMode::U);
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] == 2'b01) {
      xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]PrivilegeMode::S);
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] == 2'b11) {
      xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]PrivilegeMode::M);
    }
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] = xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::U) ? 2'b00 : 2'b11;
  }
  $pc = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mepc[CSR[mepc]]].sw_read();
} else {
  XReg qc_mcause_val_masked = qc_mcause_new_val & ~(32'b1 << 26) & ~(32'b1 << 28) & ~(32'b1 << 30) & ~(32'b1111 << 12) & ~(32'b1111 << 20);
  Bits<1> mnpie_val = (qc_mcause_val >> 28) & 1;
  Bits<4> mnpil_val = (qc_mcause_val >> 20) & 0xF;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MIE[MIE] = mnpie_val;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-NMIE[NMIE] = 1'b1;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mcause[CSR[qc.mcause]]].sw_write(qc_mcause_val_masked | (32'b1 << 28) | (mnpie_val pass:[`]<< 26) | (32'b1 << 30) | (mnpil_val pass:[`]<< 12) | (32'b1111 << 20));
  if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-MNPP[MNPP] != 2'b11) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPRV[MPRV] = 0;
    if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Smdbltrp)) {
      CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatush[mstatush]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatush-MDT[MDT] = 1'b0;
    }
  }
  if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-MNPP[MNPP] == 2'b00) {
    xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]PrivilegeMode::U);
  } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-MNPP[MNPP] == 2'b01) {
    xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]PrivilegeMode::S);
  } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-MNPP[MNPP] == 2'b11) {
    xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]PrivilegeMode::M);
  }
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnstatus[mnstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mnstatus-MNPP[MNPP] = xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::U) ? 2'b00 : 2'b11;
  $pc = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mnepc[CSR[mnepc]]].sw_read();
}

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_muliadd]
= qc.c.muliadd

Synopsis::
Multiply and accumulate (Immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.muliadd rd, rs1, uimm
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":2,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":3,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": "uimm[0|4]","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "uimm[3:1]","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Increments `rd` by the multiplication of `rs1` and an unsigned immediate
Instruction encoded in CL instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----

Bits<3> rs1 = $encoding[9:7];
Bits<3> rd = $encoding[4:2];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg reg = xref:#udb-function-creg2reg[creg2reg]pass:[(]rd);
XReg src = xref:#udb-function-creg2reg[creg2reg]pass:[(]rs1);
XReg orig_val = X[reg];
X[reg] = orig_val pass:[+] (X[src] * uimm);
----

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_mveqz]
= qc.c.mveqz

Synopsis::
Conditional Move if equal to zero

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.mveqz rd, rs1
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":2,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":3,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":3,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":6,"name": 0x2b,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Move `rs1` to `rd` if `rd` == 0, keep `rd` value otherwise
Instruction encoded in CL instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<3> rs1 = $encoding[9:7];
Bits<3> rd = $encoding[4:2];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg reg = xref:#udb-function-creg2reg[creg2reg]pass:[(]rd);
XReg src = xref:#udb-function-creg2reg[creg2reg]pass:[(]rs1);
XReg orig_val = X[reg];
X[reg] = (orig_val == 0) ? X[src] : orig_val;
----

| *Xqcicm*
| = 0.2.0

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_sync]
= qc.c.sync

Synopsis::
Non-memory-mapped device read-after-write synchronization to completion

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.sync slist
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":3,"name": "slist","type":4},{"bits":6,"name": 0x20,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
This synchronization instruction delays execution till last read (input)
from non-memory-mapped device transactions are completed for specified devices.
As well, instruction implies fence.tso functionality for all memory accesses.
Immediate argument is 3-bit encoding of 5-bit bitmask field
that specifies up to five pre-defined devices.
Values of bitmask encoding supported:  0,1,2,4,8,16,15,31
Instruction encoded in CB instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<3> slist = $encoding[9:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> bitmask;
if pass:[(]slist == 0) {
  bitmask = 0;
} else if pass:[(]slist < 6) {
  XReg shift = slist - 1;
  bitmask = (5'b1 << shift);
} else {
  XReg shift = slist - 2;
  bitmask = (5'b1 << shift) - 1;
}
xref:#udb-function-fence_tso[fence_tso]pass:[(]);
xref:#udb-function-sync_read_after_write_device[sync_read_after_write_device]pass:[(]true, bitmask);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_sync[`qc.c.sync`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0


















| *Xqcisync*
| = 0.3.0

|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_c_syncr]
= qc.c.syncr

Synopsis::
Non-memory-mapped device read-after-write synchronization

Mnemonic::
----
qc.c.syncr slist
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":3,"name": "slist","type":4},{"bits":6,"name": 0x21,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
This synchronization instruction delays execution till last read (input)
from non-memory-mapped device transactions are started for specified devices.
As well, instruction implies fence.tso functionality for all memory accesses.
Immediate argument is 3-bit encoding of 5-bit bitmask field
that specifies up to five pre-defined devices.
Values of bitmask encoding supported:  0,1,2,4,8,16,15,31
Instruction encoded in CB instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<3> slist = $encoding[9:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> bitmask;
if pass:[(]slist == 0) {
  bitmask = 0;
} else if pass:[(]slist < 6) {
  XReg shift = slist - 1;
  bitmask = (5'b1 << shift);
} else {
  XReg shift = slist - 2;
  bitmask = (5'b1 << shift) - 1;
}
xref:#udb-function-fence_tso[fence_tso]pass:[(]);
xref:#udb-function-sync_read_after_write_device[sync_read_after_write_device]pass:[(]false, bitmask);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_c_syncr[`qc.c.syncr`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0


















| *Xqcisync*
| = 0.3.0

|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_clo]
= qc.clo

Synopsis::
Count leading ones

Mnemonic::
----
qc.clo rd, rs1
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x80,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Count the number of ones before the first zero in `rs1`, starting from the MSB
and progressing to the LSB.
Accordingly, if the input is ~0, the output is XLEN, and if the most-significant
bit of the input is a 0, the output is 0.
output written to the `rd`
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
X[rd] = (xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1) - $signed+++(+++xref:#udb-function-highest_set_bit[highest_set_bit]pass:[(]~X[rs1]));
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_clo[`qc.clo`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

--

xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_write[csr_sw_write]pass:[(]pre_csr, xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_read[csr_sw_read]pass:[(]pre_csr) & ~(32'b1 << bit));

X[rd] = {16'b0, b1[7:0], b0[7:0]};

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_csrrwr]
= qc.csrrwr

Synopsis::
Atomic Read/Write CSR (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.csrrwr rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x73,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x46,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Atomically swap values in the CSRs and integer registers.
Read the old value of the CSR, zero-extends the value to `XLEN` bits,
and then write it to integer register `rd`.
The CSR number is in `rs2` register.
The initial value in `rs1` is written to the CSR.
If `rd`=`x0`, then the instruction shall not read the CSR and shall not
cause any of the side effects that might occur on a CSR read.
If `rs1`=`x0`, then the instruction shall not write to the CSR and shall not
cause any of the side effects that might occur on a CSR write.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg csr_addr = X[rs2];
Csr csr = xref:#udb-function-direct_csr_lookup[direct_csr_lookup]pass:[(]csr_addr);
if pass:[(]rd != 0) {
  X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_read[csr_sw_read]pass:[(]csr);
}
if pass:[(]rs1 != 0) {
  xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_write[csr_sw_write]pass:[(]csr, X[rs1]);
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_csrrwr[`qc.csrrwr`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0








| *Xqcicsr*
| = 0.4.0











|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_csrrwri]
= qc.csrrwri

Synopsis::
Atomic Read/Write CSR (Register) Immediate

Mnemonic::
----
qc.csrrwri rd, imm, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x73,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "imm","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x47,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Atomically write CSR using a 5-bit immediate `imm`, and load the previous value into `rd`.
Read the old value of the CSR, zero-extends the value to `XLEN` bits,
and then write it to integer register `rd`.
The CSR number is in `rs2` register.
The 5-bit uimm field is zero-extended and written to the CSR.
If `rd`=`x0`, then the instruction shall not read the CSR and shall not
cause any of the side effects that might occur on a CSR read.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> imm = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg csr_addr = X[rs2];
Csr csr = xref:#udb-function-direct_csr_lookup[direct_csr_lookup]pass:[(]csr_addr);
if pass:[(]rd != 0) {
  X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_read[csr_sw_read]pass:[(]csr);
}
xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_write[csr_sw_write]pass:[(]csr, {{MXLEN - 5{1'b0}}, imm});
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_csrrwri[`qc.csrrwri`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0








| *Xqcicsr*
| = 0.4.0











|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_e_beqi]
= qc.e.beqi

Synopsis::
Branch on equal (immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.e.beqi rs1, imm, offset
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x1f,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "offset[4:1|11]","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x4,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": 0x18,"type":2},{"bits":7,"name": "offset[12|10:5]","type":4},{"bits":16,"name": "imm != 0","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Branches to `PC` + `offset` if the value in `rs1` is equal to the signed immediate `imm`
Instruction encoded in QC.EB instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
signed Bits<13> offset = sext({$encoding[31], $encoding[7], $encoding[30:25], $encoding[11:8], 1'd0}, 13);
Bits<16> imm = $encoding[47:32];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++X[rs1]) == $signed+++(+++imm)) {
  xref:#udb-function-jump_halfword[jump_halfword]pass:[(]$pc pass:[+] $signed+++(+++offset));
}
----

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_e_lb]
= qc.e.lb

Synopsis::
Load byte

Mnemonic::
----
qc.e.lb rd, imm(rs1)
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x1f,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x5,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":10,"name": "imm[9:0]","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":16,"name": "imm[25:10]","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Load 8 bits of data into register `rd` from an
address formed by adding `rs1` to a signed offset `imm`.
Sign extend the result.
Instruction encoded in QC.EI instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<26> imm = {$encoding[47:32], $encoding[29:20]};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg virtual_address = X[rs1] pass:[+] $signed+++(+++imm);
X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]8, virtual_address, $encoding), 8);
----


Included in::

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0














| *Xqcilo*
| = 0.3.0





|===

and store the result in `rd`.

Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<26> imm = {$encoding[47:32], $encoding[29:20]};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
X[rd] = X[rs1] | xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(]imm, 26);
----


Included in::

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0













| *Xqcilia*
| = 0.2.0






|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_expand2]
= qc.expand2

Synopsis::
Bit expansion (every 2nd bit)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.expand2 rd, rs1
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x40,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Bit expansion (every 2nd bit) of `rs1`, bits [31:16] of `rs1` are ignored.
Write result to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.

Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg b0 = {X[rs1][3], X[rs1][3], X[rs1][2], X[rs1][2], X[rs1][1], X[rs1][1], X[rs1][0], X[rs1][0]};
XReg b1 = {X[rs1][7], X[rs1][7], X[rs1][6], X[rs1][6], X[rs1][5], X[rs1][5], X[rs1][4], X[rs1][4]};
XReg b2 = {X[rs1][11], X[rs1][11], X[rs1][10], X[rs1][10], X[rs1][9], X[rs1][9], X[rs1][8], X[rs1][8]};
XReg b3 = {X[rs1][15], X[rs1][15], X[rs1][14], X[rs1][14], X[rs1][13], X[rs1][13], X[rs1][12], X[rs1][12]};
X[rd] = {b3[7:0], b2[7:0], b1[7:0], b0[7:0]};
----
