[#udb:doc:inst:qc_ext]
= qc.ext

Synopsis::
Extract bits signed

Mnemonic::
----
qc.ext rd, rs1, width, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "shamt","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "width_minus1","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Extract a subset of bits from `rs1` into `rd`, and sign-extend the result.
The width of the subset is determined by (`width_minus1` + 1) (1..32),
and the offset of the subset is determined by `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> width_minus1 = $encoding[29:25];
Bits<5> shamt = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg width = width_minus1 pass:[+] 1;
XReg unsigned_extraction = (X[rs1] >> shamt) & ((32'b1 << width) - 1);
X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(]unsigned_extraction, width);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_ext[`qc.ext`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_extd]
= qc.extd

Synopsis::
Extract bits from pair signed (Immediate)

qc.extd rd, rs1, width, shamt

....

Description::
Extract a subset of bits from the register pair [`rs1`, `rs1`+1] into `rd`, and sign extend the result.
The width of the subset is determined by (`width_minus1` + 1) (1..32),
and the offset (into the pair) of the subset is determined by `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.

Bits<5> width_minus1 = $encoding[29:25];
Bits<5> shamt = $encoding[24:20];

Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<{1'b0, MXLEN} * 2> pair = {X[rs1 pass:[+] 1], X[rs1]};
XReg width = width_minus1 pass:[+] 1;
X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(](pair >> shamt) & ((32'b1 << width) - 1), width);
----


Included in::

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_extdpr]
= qc.extdpr

Synopsis::
Extract bits from pair signed, packed descriptor (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.extdpr rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 31","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x8,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Extract a subset of bits from the register pair [`rs1`, `rs1`+1] into `rd`, and sign extend the result.
The width of the subset is determined by `rs2` bits [13:8] (0..32),
and the offset of the subset is determined by `rs2` bits [5:0] (0..63).
In case when `rs2` bit [13] == 1 width is enforced to 32.
In case when width == 0, to the destination register written 0.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<{1'b0, MXLEN} * 2> pair = {X[rs1 pass:[+] 1], X[rs1]};
XReg width_bits = X[rs2][13:8];
XReg width = (width_bits > 32) ? 32 : width_bits;
XReg shamt = X[rs2][5:0];
if pass:[(]width > 0) {
  X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(](pair >> shamt) & ((32'b1 << width) - 1), width);
} else {
  X[rd] = 0;
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_extdpr[`qc.extdpr`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2

Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<{1'b0, MXLEN} * 2> pair = {X[rs1 pass:[+] 1], X[rs1]};
XReg width = width_minus1 pass:[+] 1;
X[rd] = (pair >> shamt) & ((32'b1 << width) - 1);
----


Included in::

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0

<<<

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_extdupr]
= qc.extdupr

Synopsis::
Extract bits from pair unsigned, packed descriptor (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.extdupr rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 31","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x6,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Extract a subset of bits from the register pair [`rs1`, `rs1`+1] into `rd`.
The width of the subset is determined by `rs2` bits [13:8] (0..32),
and the offset of the subset is determined by `rs2` bits [5:0] (0..63).
In case when `rs2` bit [13] == 1 width is enforced to 32.
In case when width == 0, to the destination register written 0.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<{1'b0, MXLEN} * 2> pair = {X[rs1 pass:[+] 1], X[rs1]};
XReg width_bits = X[rs2][13:8];
XReg width = (width_bits > 32) ? 32 : width_bits;
XReg shamt = X[rs2][5:0];
if pass:[(]width > 0) {
  X[rd] = (pair >> shamt) & ((32'b1 << width) - 1);
} else {
  X[rd] = 0;
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_extdupr[`qc.extdupr`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_insb]
= qc.insb

Synopsis::
Insert bits (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.insb rd, rs1, width, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "shamt","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "width_minus1","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Insertion of a subset of bits from `rs1` into `rd`.
The width of the subset is determined by (`width_minus1` + 1) (1..32),
and the offset of the subset is determined by `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> width_minus1 = $encoding[29:25];
Bits<5> shamt = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg width = width_minus1 pass:[+] 1;
XReg mask = ((32'b1 << width) - 1) << shamt;
XReg orig_val = X[rd];
X[rd] = (orig_val & ~mask) | ((X[rs1] << shamt) & mask);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_insb[`qc.insb`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_insbh]
= qc.insbh

Synopsis::
Insert bits in 64-bit higher part (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.insbh rd, rs1, width, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "shamt","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "width_minus1","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x2,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Insertion of a subset of bits from `rs1` into `rd`.
Instruction intended for insertion bits into bitfield within 64-bits,
when bitfield crosses 32-bit bundary.
Lower part of 64-bit destination is inserted using QC32.INSB,
higher part using QC32.INSBH.
The width of the subset is determined by (`width_minus1` + 1) (1..32),
and the offset of the subset is determined by `shamt`.
In case when width + offset < 33, the destination register is left unchanged.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> width_minus1 = $encoding[29:25];
Bits<5> shamt = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg width = width_minus1 pass:[+] 1;
if pass:[(]width pass:[+] shamt > 32) {
  XReg shifted_one = 32'b1 << (width pass:[+] shamt - 32);
  XReg mask = (shifted_one - 1);
  XReg orig_val = X[rd];
  XReg shifted_rs1 = X[rs1] >> (32 - shamt);
  X[rd] = (orig_val & ~mask) | (shifted_rs1 & mask);
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_insbh[`qc.insbh`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_insbhr]
= qc.insbhr

Synopsis::
Insert bits in 64-bit higher part (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.insbhr rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x1,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Insertion of a subset of bits from `rs1` into `rd`.
Instruction intended for insertion bits into bitfield within 64-bits,
when bitfield crosses 32-bit bundary.
Lower part of 64-bit destination is inserted using QC32.INSBR,
higher part using QC32.INSBHR.
The width of the subset is determined by `rs2` bits [21:16] (0..32),
and the offset of the subset is determined by `rs2` bits [4:0].
In case when width + offset < 33 or width == 0, the destination register is left unchanged.
In case when `rs2` bit [21] == 1 width is enforced to 32.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg width_bits = X[rs2][21:16];
XReg width = (width_bits > 32) ? 32 : width_bits;
XReg shamt = X[rs2][4:0];
if pass:[(](width pass:[+] shamt > 32) && (width > 0)) {
  XReg shifted_one = 32'b1 << (width pass:[+] shamt - 32);
  XReg mask = (shifted_one - 1);
  XReg orig_val = X[rd];
  XReg shifted_rs1 = X[rs1] >> (32 - shamt);
  X[rd] = (orig_val & ~mask) | (shifted_rs1 & mask);
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_insbhr[`qc.insbhr`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0




| *Xqcibm*
| = 0.8.0















|===

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_inw]
= qc.inw

Synopsis::
Input word from non-memory-mapped device

Mnemonic::
----
qc.inw rd, imm(rs1)
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x5,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": "imm[13:2]","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Input 32 bits of data into register `rd` from a non-memory-mapped device.
Such devices have own address space, unrelated to memory map.
Device space address formed by adding `rs1` to  to a unsigned offset `imm`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<14> imm = {$encoding[31:20], 2'd0};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg device_address = X[rs1] pass:[+] imm;
X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-read_device_32[read_device_32]pass:[(]device_address);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_inw[`qc.inw`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0










| *Xqciio*
| any









|===

--

....

Description::

----

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_lieq]
= qc.lieq

Synopsis::
Conditional load immediate if equal (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.lieq rd, rs1, rs2, simm
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x5b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x1,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "simm","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Move `simm` to `rd` if the value in `rs1` is equal to value `rs2`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> simm = $encoding[31:27];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]X[rs1] == X[rs2]) {
  X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(]simm, 5);
}
----


Included in::

| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0





| *Xqcicli*
| = 0.3.0














|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_lrb]
= qc.lrb

Synopsis::
Load indexed byte

Mnemonic::
----
qc.lrb rd, rs1, rs2, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x7,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "shamt","type":4},{"bits":4,"name": 0x8,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Load 8 bits of data into register `rd` from an
address formed by adding `rs1` to `rs2`, shifted by `shamt`.
Sign extend the result.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<3> shamt = $encoding[27:25];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg virtual_address = X[rs1] pass:[+] (X[rs2] << shamt);
X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-sext[sext]pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]8, virtual_address, $encoding), 8);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_lrb[`qc.lrb`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

















| *Xqcisls*
| = 0.2.0


|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_lrbu]
= qc.lrbu

Synopsis::
Load indexed unsigned byte

Mnemonic::
----
qc.lrbu rd, rs1, rs2, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x7,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "shamt","type":4},{"bits":4,"name": 0xb,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Load 8 bits of data into register `rd` from an
address formed by adding `rs1` to `rs2`, shifted by `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<3> shamt = $encoding[27:25];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg virtual_address = X[rs1] pass:[+] (X[rs2] << shamt);
X[rd] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]8, virtual_address, $encoding);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_lrbu[`qc.lrbu`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

















| *Xqcisls*
| = 0.2.0


|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_lwm]
= qc.lwm

Synopsis::
Load word multiple

Mnemonic::
----
qc.lwm rd, rs2, imm(rs1)
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x7,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "imm[6:2]","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Loads multiple words starting from address (`rs1` + `imm`) to registers, starting from `rd`.
The number of words is in `rs2` bits [4:0].
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<7> imm = {$encoding[29:25], 2'd0};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg vaddr = X[rs1] pass:[+] imm;
XReg num_words = X[rs2][4:0];
xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), $encoding) if (((rd pass:[+] num_words) > 32));
for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < num_words; i++) {
  X[rd pass:[+] i] = xref:#udb-function-read_memory[read_memory]pass:[(]32, vaddr, $encoding);
  vaddr = vaddr pass:[+] 4;
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_lwm[`qc.lwm`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0















| *Xqcilsm*
| = 0.6.0




|===

if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++X[rs1]) < $signed+++(+++imm)) {
  X[rd] = X[rs3];
}
----

| = 0.13.0






| *Xqcicm*
| = 0.2.0

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_mvltu]
= qc.mvltu

Synopsis::
Conditional move if less than unsigned (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.mvltu rd, rs1, rs2, rs3
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x5b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x6,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs3 != 0","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Move `rs3` to `rd` if the unsigned value in `rs1` is less than unsigned value `rs2`.
Instruction encoded in R4 instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs3 = $encoding[31:27];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]X[rs1] < X[rs2]) {
  X[rd] = X[rs3];
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_mvltu[`qc.mvltu`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0






| *Xqcicm*
| = 0.2.0













|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_norm]
= qc.norm

Synopsis::
Signed Normalization

Mnemonic::
----
qc.norm rd, rs1
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0xe0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Signed normalization of `rs1`.
Exponent written in bits[7:0] of the result.
Mantissa written in bits[31:8] of the result.
Write result to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg clz = (xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1) - $signed+++(+++xref:#udb-function-highest_set_bit[highest_set_bit]pass:[(]X[rs1]));
XReg clo = (xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1) - $signed+++(+++xref:#udb-function-highest_set_bit[highest_set_bit]pass:[(]~X[rs1]));
XReg mnt = (X[rs1][31] == 1) ? (X[rs1] << (clo - 1)) : (X[rs1] << (clz - 1));
XReg exp = (X[rs1][31] == 1) ? (-(clo - 1)) : (-(clz - 1));
X[rd] = {mnt[31:8], exp[7:0]};
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_norm[`qc.norm`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_normeu]
= qc.normeu

Synopsis::
Unsigned Even Normalization

Mnemonic::
----
qc.normeu rd, rs1
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": 0x120,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Unsigned even normalization of `rs1` (exponent is even).
Even exponent written in bits[7:0] of the result.
Mantissa (based on even exponent) written in bits[31:8] of the result.
Write result to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg clz = ((xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1) - $signed+++(+++xref:#udb-function-highest_set_bit[highest_set_bit]pass:[(]X[rs1]))) & ~1;
XReg mnt = (X[rs1] << (clz & ~1));
XReg exp = (-(clz & ~1));
X[rd] = {mnt[31:8], exp[7:0]};
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_normeu[`qc.normeu`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_outw]
= qc.outw

Synopsis::
Output word to non-memory-mapped device

Mnemonic::
----
qc.outw rs2, imm(rs1)
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x4,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":12,"name": "imm[13:2]","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Output 32 bits of data from register `rs2` to a non-memory-mapped device.
Such devices have own address space, unrelated to memory map.
Device space address formed by adding `rs1` to  to a unsigned offset `imm`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<14> imm = {$encoding[31:20], 2'd0};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg device_address = X[rs1] pass:[+] imm;
xref:#udb-function-write_device_32[write_device_32]pass:[(]device_address, X[rs2]);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_outw[`qc.outw`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0










| *Xqciio*
| any









|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_pcoredump]
= qc.pcoredump

Synopsis::
Print core dump pseudo-instruction (hint) working only in simulation environment

Mnemonic::
----
qc.pcoredump 
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":32,"name": 0x60002013,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
The print core dump instruction calls simulation environment with no explicit arguments.
Implicit arguments are all general purpose registers and CSRs.
Simulation environment expected to print the core dump on its console or standard output.
The core dump format and content are defined by simulation environment.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::


qc.pcoredump has no decode variables.



Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg func = 8;
XReg arg = 0;
xref:#udb-function-iss_syscall[iss_syscall]pass:[(]func, arg);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_pcoredump[`qc.pcoredump`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0
















| *Xqcisim*
| = 0.2.0



|===

Additional implicit arguments defined by simulation environment implementation.
Instruction is used to call simulator to execute function according to the argument.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<10> imm = $encoding[29:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg func = 11;
XReg arg = imm;
xref:#udb-function-iss_syscall[iss_syscall]pass:[(]func, arg);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_psyscalli[`qc.psyscalli`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0
















| *Xqcisim*
| = 0.2.0



|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_selecteqi]
= qc.selecteqi

Synopsis::
Select load immediate or register if equal (Immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.selecteqi rd, imm, rs2, rs3
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x5b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "imm","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x2,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs3 != 0","type":4}]}
....

Description::
Move `rs2` to `rd` if the value in `rd` is equal to value `imm`,
move `rs3` to `rd` otherwise.
Instruction encoded in R4 instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> imm = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs3 = $encoding[31:27];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++X[rd]) == $signed+++(+++imm)) {
  X[rd] = X[rs2];
} else {
  X[rd] = X[rs3];
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_selecteqi[`qc.selecteqi`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0







| *Xqcics*
| = 0.2.0












|===

Csr pre_csr = xref:#udb-function-direct_csr_lookup[direct_csr_lookup]pass:[(]MCLICIP0_ADDR pass:[+] idx);
xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_write[csr_sw_write]pass:[(]pre_csr, xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_read[csr_sw_read]pass:[(]pre_csr) | (32'b1 << bit));

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_setwm]
= qc.setwm

Synopsis::
Set word multiple (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.setwm rs3, rs2, imm(rs1)
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs3","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x7,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "imm[6:2]","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x2,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Stores the value of `rs3` multiple times into the address starting at (`rs1` + `imm`).
The number of writes is in `rs2` bits [4:0] (0..31).
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<7> imm = {$encoding[29:25], 2'd0};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs3 = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg vaddr = X[rs1] pass:[+] imm;
Bits<32> write_value = X[rs3][31:0];
XReg num_words = X[rs2][4:0];
for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < num_words; i++) {
  xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, vaddr, write_value, $encoding);
  vaddr = vaddr pass:[+] 4;
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_setwm[`qc.setwm`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0















| *Xqcilsm*
| = 0.6.0




|===

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_shlsat]
= qc.shlsat

Synopsis::
Saturating signed left shift

Mnemonic::
----
qc.shlsat rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xa,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Left shift `rs1` by the value of `rs2`, and saturate the signed result.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> sext_double_width_rs1 = {{xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]){X[rs1][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1]}}, X[rs1]};
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> shifted_value = sext_double_width_rs1 << X[rs2][4:0];
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> most_negative_number = {{(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) pass:[+] 1){1'b1}}, {(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1){1'b0}}};
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> most_positive_number = {{(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) pass:[+] 1){1'b0}}, {(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1){1'b1}}};
if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++shifted_value) < $signed+++(+++most_negative_number)) {
  X[rd] = most_negative_number[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
} else if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++shifted_value) > $signed+++(+++most_positive_number)) {
  X[rd] = most_positive_number[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
} else {
  X[rd] = shifted_value[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_shlsat[`qc.shlsat`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_shlusat]
= qc.shlusat

Synopsis::
Saturating unsigned left shift

Mnemonic::
----
qc.shlusat rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0xc,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Left shift `rs1` by the value of `rs2`, and saturate the unsigned result.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> zext_double_width_rs1 = {{xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]){1'b0}}, X[rs1]};
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> shifted_value = zext_double_width_rs1 << X[rs2][4:0];
Bits<MXLEN pass:[`]* 2> largest_unsigned_value = {{xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]){1'b0}}, {xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]){1'b1}}};
if pass:[(]shifted_value > largest_unsigned_value) {
  X[rd] = largest_unsigned_value[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
} else {
  X[rd] = shifted_value[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_shlusat[`qc.shlusat`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_srb]
= qc.srb

Synopsis::
Store indexed byte

Mnemonic::
----
qc.srb rs3, rs1, rs2, shamt
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs3","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x6,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": "shamt","type":4},{"bits":4,"name": 0xd,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Store 8 bits of data from register `rs3` to an
address formed by adding `rs1` to `rs2`, shifted by `shamt`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<3> shamt = $encoding[27:25];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs3 = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg virtual_address = X[rs1] pass:[+] (X[rs2] << shamt);
xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]8, virtual_address, X[rs3][7:0], $encoding);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_srb[`qc.srb`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

















| *Xqcisls*
| = 0.2.0


|===

--

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_subsat]
= qc.subsat

Synopsis::
Saturating signed subtraction

Mnemonic::
----
qc.subsat rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x10,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Subtract signed values `rs1` and `rs2`, saturate the signed result, and write to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> result = X[rs1] pass:[`]- X[rs2];
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> most_negative_number = {2'b11, {(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1){1'b0}}};
Bits<MXLEN pass:[+] 1> most_positive_number = {2'b00, {(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1){1'b1}}};
if pass:[(]X[rs1][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1] != X[rs2][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1]) {
  if pass:[(]result[xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1] != X[rs1][xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1]) {
    if pass:[(]$signed+++(+++X[rs1]) < 's0) {
      result = most_negative_number;
    } else {
      result = most_positive_number;
    }
  }
}
X[rd] = result[(xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1):0];
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_subsat[`qc.subsat`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

= qc.subusat

Synopsis::
Saturating unsigned subtraction

Mnemonic::
----
qc.subusat rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x11,"type":2}]}
....

Subtract unsigned values `rs1` and `rs2`, saturate the unsigned result, and write to `rd`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
X[rd] = (X[rs1] < X[rs2]) ? 0 : X[rs1] - X[rs2];
----

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_swm]
= qc.swm

Synopsis::
Store word multiple

Mnemonic::
----
qc.swm rs3, rs2, imm(rs1)
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0x2b,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs3 != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x7,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "imm[6:2]","type":4},{"bits":2,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
Stores multiple words from the registers starting at `rs3` to the address starting at (`rs1` + `imm`).
The number of words is in `rs2` bits [4:0].
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<7> imm = {$encoding[29:25], 2'd0};
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rs3 = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg vaddr = X[rs1] pass:[+] imm;
XReg num_words = X[rs2][4:0];
xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), $encoding) if (((rs3 pass:[+] num_words) > 32));
for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < num_words; i++) {
  xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, vaddr, X[rs3 pass:[+] i], $encoding);
  vaddr = vaddr pass:[+] 4;
}
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_swm[`qc.swm`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0















| *Xqcilsm*
| = 0.6.0




|===

--

  xref:#udb-function-write_memory[write_memory]pass:[(]32, vaddr, X[rs3 pass:[+] i], $encoding);

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_sync]
= qc.sync

Synopsis::
Non-memory-mapped device read-after-write synchronization to completion

Mnemonic::
----
qc.sync imm
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":20,"name": 0x3013,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "imm","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x8,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
This synchronization instruction delays execution till last read (input)
from non-memory-mapped device transactions are completed for specified devices.
As well, instruction implies fence.tso functionality for all memory accesses.
Immediate argument is 5-bit bitmask field that specifies up to five pre-defined devices.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> imm = $encoding[24:20];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
xref:#udb-function-fence_tso[fence_tso]pass:[(]);
xref:#udb-function-sync_read_after_write_device[sync_read_after_write_device]pass:[(]true, imm);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_sync[`qc.sync`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0


















| *Xqcisync*
| = 0.3.0

|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2

[#udb:doc:inst:qc_wrap]
= qc.wrap

Synopsis::
Wraparound (Register)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.wrap rd, rs1, rs2
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x3,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1","type":4},{"bits":5,"name": "rs2 != 0","type":4},{"bits":7,"name": 0x12,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
If `rs1` >= `rs2` perform subtraction between `rs1` and `rs2`.
If `rs1` < 0, perform addition between `rs1` and `rs2`,
else, select `rs1`. The result is stored in `rd`.
Instruction encoded in R instruction format.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rs2 = $encoding[24:20];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg rs1_value = X[rs1];
X[rd] = ($signed+++(+++rs1_value) >= $signed+++(+++X[rs2])) ? rs1_value - X[rs2] : (($signed+++(+++rs1_value) < 's0) ? (rs1_value pass:[+] X[rs2]) : rs1_value);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_wrap[`qc.wrap`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<
:leveloffset: +2


[#udb:doc:inst:qc_wrapi]
= qc.wrapi

Synopsis::
Wraparound (Unsigned Immediate)

Mnemonic::
----
qc.wrapi rd, rs1, imm
----

Encoding::
[wavedrom, ,svg,subs='attributes',width="100%"]
....
{"reg":[{"bits":7,"name": 0xb,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rd != 0","type":4},{"bits":3,"name": 0x0,"type":2},{"bits":5,"name": "rs1 != 0","type":4},{"bits":11,"name": "imm","type":4},{"bits":1,"name": 0x0,"type":2}]}
....

Description::
If `rs1` >= `imm` perform subtraction between `rs1` and `imm`.
If `rs1` < 0, perform addition between `rs1` and `imm`,
else, select `rs1`. The result is stored in `rd`.
Instruction encoded in I instruction format.
The `imm` is an unsigned immediate.



Decode Variables::

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<11> imm = $encoding[30:20];
Bits<5> rs1 = $encoding[19:15];
Bits<5> rd = $encoding[11:7];
----


Operation::
[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg rs1_value = X[rs1];
X[rd] = ($signed+++(+++rs1_value) >= $signed+++(+++{1'b0, imm})) ? rs1_value - imm : (($signed+++(+++rs1_value) < 's0) ? ($signed+++(+++rs1_value) pass:[+] imm) : rs1_value);
----


Included in::
--
xref:#udb-insn-qc_wrapi[`qc.wrapi`] is unconditionally defined by the following:

|===
| Extension | Version

| *Xqci*
| = 0.13.0

| *Xqcia*
| = 0.7.0


















|===

--

:leveloffset: -2

<<<

<<<
== IDL Functions

[#udb-function-abort_current_instruction]
=== abort_current_instruction (builtin)
Abort the current instruction, and start refetching from $pc.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

None

|===


[#udb-function-access_check]
=== access_check
Checks if the physical address paddr is able to access memory, and raises
the appropriate exception if not.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH>`
! paddr
! 1
h! `U32`
! access_size
! 2
h! `XReg`
! vaddr
! 3
h! `MemoryOperation`
! type
! 4
h! `ExceptionCode`
! fault_type
! 5
h! `PrivilegeMode`
! from_mode
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]paddr > ((1 pass:[`]<< PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH) - access_size)) {
  xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]fault_type, from_mode, vaddr);
}
if pass:[(]NUM_PMP_ENTRIES > 0) {
  if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-pmp_check[pmp_check]pass:[(]paddr[PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 1:0], access_size, type)) {
    xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]fault_type, from_mode, vaddr);
  }
}
----

[#udb-function-creg2reg]
=== creg2reg
Maps a C register index (_e.g._, `rs1'` in the specification) to an X register index. From the
specification:

.Registers specified by the three-bit _rs1_&#x2032;, _rs2_&#x2032;, and _rd_&#x2032; fields of the CIW, CL, CS, CA, and CB formats.
//[cols="20%,10%,10%,10%,10%,10%,10%,10%,10%"]

[#udb-function-current_translation_mode]
=== current_translation_mode
Returns the current first-stage translation mode for an explicit load or store
from +mode+ given the machine state (e.g., value of `satp` or `vsatp` csr).

Returns SatpMode::Reserved if the setting found in `satp` or `vsatp` is invalid.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `SatpMode`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `PrivilegeMode`
! mode
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
PrivilegeMode effective_mode = xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]);
if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::M) {
  return SatpMode::Bare;
}
if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-H[H] == 1'b1) {
  if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS || effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU) {
    Bits<4> mode_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsatp[vsatp]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsatp-MODE[MODE];
    if pass:[(]mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Bare)) {
      return SatpMode::Bare;
    } else if pass:[(]mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv32)) {
      if pass:[(]MXLEN == 64) {
        if pass:[(](effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS) && (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-VSXL[VSXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32))) {
          return SatpMode::Reserved;
        }
        if pass:[(](effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU) && (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32))) {
          return SatpMode::Reserved;
        }
      }
      if pass:[(]!SV32_VSMODE_TRANSLATION) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      return SatpMode::Sv32;
    } else if pass:[(](MXLEN == 64) && (mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv39))) {
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-VSXL[VSXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]!SV39_VSMODE_TRANSLATION) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      return SatpMode::Sv39;
    } else if pass:[(](MXLEN == 64) && (mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv48))) {
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-VSXL[VSXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]!SV48_VSMODE_TRANSLATION) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      return SatpMode::Sv48;
    } else if pass:[(](MXLEN == 64) && (mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv57))) {
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-VSXL[VSXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]!SV57_VSMODE_TRANSLATION) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      return SatpMode::Sv57;
    } else {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
  } else {
    return SatpMode::Reserved;
  }
} else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1'b1) {
  xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::S || effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::U, "unexpected priv mode");
  Bits<4> mode_val = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-satp[satp]].xref:#udb-csrfield-satp-MODE[MODE];
  if pass:[(]mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Bare)) {
    return SatpMode::Bare;
  } else if pass:[(]mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv32)) {
    if pass:[(]MXLEN == 64) {
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::S && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SXL[SXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
      if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::U && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-sstatus[sstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-sstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
        return SatpMode::Reserved;
      }
    }
    if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Sv32)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    return SatpMode::Sv32;
  } else if pass:[(](MXLEN == 64) && (mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv39))) {
    if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::S && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SXL[SXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::U && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-sstatus[sstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-sstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Sv39)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    return SatpMode::Sv39;
  } else if pass:[(](MXLEN == 64) && (mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv48))) {
    if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::S && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SXL[SXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::U && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-sstatus[sstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-sstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Sv48)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    return SatpMode::Sv48;
  } else if pass:[(](MXLEN == 64) && (mode_val == $bits(SatpMode::Sv57))) {
    if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::S && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SXL[SXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::U && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-sstatus[sstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-sstatus-UXL[UXL] != $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Sv57)) {
      return SatpMode::Reserved;
    }
    return SatpMode::Sv57;
  } else {
    return SatpMode::Reserved;
  }
} else {
  return SatpMode::Reserved;
}
----

[#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode]
=== effective_ldst_mode
Returns the effective privilege mode for normal explicit loads and stores, taking into account
the current actual privilege mode and modifications from xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPRV[`mstatus.MPRV`].
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `PrivilegeMode`
h| Arguments
a|

None

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::M) {
  if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-U[U] == 1 && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPRV[MPRV] == 1) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] == 0b00) {
      if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::H) && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-H[H] == 1 && xref:#udb-function-mpv[mpv]pass:[(]) == 0b1) {
        return PrivilegeMode::VU;
      } else {
        return PrivilegeMode::U;
      }
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1 && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] == 0b01) {
      if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::H) && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-H[H] == 1 && xref:#udb-function-mpv[mpv]pass:[(]) == 0b1) {
        return PrivilegeMode::VS;
      } else {
        return PrivilegeMode::S;
      }
    }
  }
}
return xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]);
----

[#udb-function-exception_handling_mode]
=== exception_handling_mode
Returns the target privilege mode that will handle synchronous exception `exception_code`
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `PrivilegeMode`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `ExceptionCode`
! exception_code
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::M) {
  return PrivilegeMode::M;
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::S) && ((xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::HS) || (xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::U))) {
  if pass:[(]($bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-medeleg[CSR[medeleg]]]) & (MXLEN'1 << $bits(exception_code))) != 0) {
    return PrivilegeMode::HS;
  } else {
    return PrivilegeMode::M;
  }
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::H) && ((xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::VS) || (xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::VU))) {
  if pass:[(]($bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-medeleg[CSR[medeleg]]]) & (MXLEN'1 << $bits(exception_code))) != 0) {
    if pass:[(]($bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hedeleg[CSR[hedeleg]]]) & (MXLEN'1 << $bits(exception_code))) != 0) {
      return PrivilegeMode::VS;
    } else {
      return PrivilegeMode::HS;
    }
  } else {
    return PrivilegeMode::M;
  }
} else {
  xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
}
----

[#udb-function-get_and_validate_stack_pointer]
=== get_and_validate_stack_pointer
Validate and return stack pointer.
Stack pointer is validated to fit in range, defined by qc.mstktopaddr and qc.mstkbottomaddr CSRs.
In case when stack pointer is out-of-range, raising exception SpOutOfRange.
Stack pointer is also validated to be 16-byte aligned.
In case when stack pointer is not 16-bytes aligned, raising exception IllegalStackPointer.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `XReg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! sp
! 1
h! `Bits<INSTR_ENC_SIZE>`
! encoding
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]sp < $bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mstkbottomaddr[CSR[qc.mstkbottomaddr]]])) {
  xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::SpOutOfRange, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), encoding);
} else if pass:[(]sp > $bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-qc_mstktopaddr[CSR[qc.mstktopaddr]]])) {
  xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::SpOutOfRange, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), encoding);
} else if pass:[(](sp & 0xf) != 0) {
  xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::IllegalStackPointer, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), encoding);
}
return sp;
----

[#udb-function-highest_set_bit]
=== highest_set_bit
Returns the position of the highest (nearest MSB) bit that is '1',
or -1 if value is zero.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Bits<8>`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! value
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
for pass:[(]Bits<8> i = xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  if pass:[(]value[i] == 1) {
    return i;
  }
}
return -'sd1;
----

[#udb-function-ialign]
=== ialign
Returns IALIGN, the smallest instruction encoding size, in bits.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Bits<6>`
h| Arguments
a|

None

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

  return 16;
} else {
  return 32;
}
----

[#udb-function-in_naturally_aligned_region?]
=== in_naturally_aligned_region?
Checks if a length-bit access starting at +address+ lies entirely within an N-bit naturally-aligned region.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Boolean`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `U32`
! N
! 1
h! `XReg`
! address
! 2
h! `U32`
! length
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
XReg Mask = (N / 8) - 1;
return (address & ~Mask) == ((address pass:[+] length - 1) & ~Mask);
----

[#udb-function-is_naturally_aligned]
=== is_naturally_aligned
Checks if value is naturally aligned to N bits.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Boolean`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `U32`
! N
! 1
h! `XReg`
! value
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
return true if (N == 8);
XReg Mask = (N / 8) - 1;
return (value & ~Mask) == value;
----

[#udb-function-jump_halfword]
=== jump_halfword
Jump to virtual halfword address `target_hw_addr`.

If target address is misaligned, raise a `MisalignedAddress` exception.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! target_hw_addr
!===

----
xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(](target_hw_addr & 0x1) == 0x0, "Expected halfword-aligned address in jump_halfword");
if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-ialign[ialign]pass:[(]) != 16) {
  if pass:[(](target_hw_addr & 0x3) != 0) {
    xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::InstructionAddressMisaligned, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), target_hw_addr);
  }
}
$pc = target_hw_addr;
----

[#udb-function-misaligned_is_atomic?]
=== misaligned_is_atomic?
Returns true if an access starting at +physical_address+ that is +N+ bits long is atomic.

This function takes into account any Atomicity Granule PMAs, so *it should not be used
for load-reserved/store-conditional*, since those PMAs do not apply to those accesses.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Boolean`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `U32`
! N
! 1
h! `Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH>`
! physical_address
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
return false if (MISALIGNED_MAX_ATOMICITY_GRANULE_SIZE == 0);
if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-pma_applies?[pma_applies?]pass:[(]PmaAttribute::MAG16, physical_address, N) && xref:#udb-function-in_naturally_aligned_region?[in_naturally_aligned_region?]pass:[(]128, physical_address, N)) {
  return true;
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-pma_applies?[pma_applies?]pass:[(]PmaAttribute::MAG8, physical_address, N) && xref:#udb-function-in_naturally_aligned_region?[in_naturally_aligned_region?]pass:[(]64, physical_address, N)) {
  return true;
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-pma_applies?[pma_applies?]pass:[(]PmaAttribute::MAG4, physical_address, N) && xref:#udb-function-in_naturally_aligned_region?[in_naturally_aligned_region?]pass:[(]32, physical_address, N)) {
  return true;
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-pma_applies?[pma_applies?]pass:[(]PmaAttribute::MAG2, physical_address, N) && xref:#udb-function-in_naturally_aligned_region?[in_naturally_aligned_region?]pass:[(]16, physical_address, N)) {
  return true;
} else {
  return false;
}
----

[#udb-function-mode]

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `PrivilegeMode`
h| Arguments

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

  return PrivilegeMode::M;
} else {
  return current_mode;
}
----

[#udb-function-mtval_for]
=== mtval_for
Given an exception code and a *legal* non-zero value for mtval,
returns the value to be written in mtval considering implementation options
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `XReg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `ExceptionCode`
! exception_code
! 1
h! `XReg`
! tval
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::Breakpoint) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_BREAKPOINT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::LoadAddressMisaligned) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_LOAD_MISALIGNED ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAddressMisaligned) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_STORE_AMO_MISALIGNED ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::InstructionAddressMisaligned) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_INSTRUCTION_MISALIGNED ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::LoadAccessFault) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_LOAD_ACCESS_FAULT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAccessFault) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_STORE_AMO_ACCESS_FAULT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::InstructionAccessFault) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_INSTRUCTION_ACCESS_FAULT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::LoadPageFault) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_LOAD_PAGE_FAULT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::StoreAmoPageFault) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_STORE_AMO_PAGE_FAULT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::InstructionPageFault) {
  return REPORT_VA_IN_MTVAL_ON_INSTRUCTION_PAGE_FAULT ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::IllegalInstruction) {
  return REPORT_ENCODING_IN_MTVAL_ON_ILLEGAL_INSTRUCTION ? tval : 0;
} else if pass:[(]exception_code == ExceptionCode::SoftwareCheck) {
  return tval;
} else {
  return 0;
}
----

[#udb-function-pmp_check]
=== pmp_check
Given a physical address and operation type, return whether or not the access is allowed by PMP.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Boolean`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH>`
! paddr
! 1
h! `U32`
! access_size
! 2
h! `MemoryOperation`
! type
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
PrivilegeMode mode = xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]);
PmpMatchResult match_result;
PmpCfg cfg;
(match_result, cfg = xref:#udb-function-pmp_match[pmp_match]pass:[(]paddr, access_size));
if pass:[(]match_result == PmpMatchResult::FullMatch) {
  if pass:[(]mode == PrivilegeMode::M && (cfg.L == 0)) {
    return true;
  }
  if pass:[(]type == MemoryOperation::Write && (cfg.W == 0)) {
    return false;
  } else if pass:[(]type == MemoryOperation::Read && (cfg.R == 0)) {
    return false;
  } else if pass:[(]type == MemoryOperation::Fetch && (cfg.X == 0)) {
    return false;
  }
} else if pass:[(]match_result == PmpMatchResult::NoMatch) {
  if pass:[(]mode == PrivilegeMode::M) {
    return true;
  } else {
    return false;
  }
} else {
  xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]match_result == PmpMatchResult::PartialMatch, "PMP matching logic error");
  return false;
}
return true;
----

[#udb-function-pmp_match]
=== pmp_match
Given a physical address, see if any PMP entry matches.

If there is a complete match, return the PmpCfg that guards the region.
If there is no match or a partial match, report that result.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `PmpMatchResult, PmpCfg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH>`
! paddr
! 1
h! `U32`
! access_size
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]MXLEN == 64) {
  return xref:#udb-function-pmp_match_64[pmp_match_64]pass:[(]paddr, access_size);
} else {
  return xref:#udb-function-pmp_match_32[pmp_match_32]pass:[(]paddr, access_size);
}
----

[#udb-function-pmp_match_32]
=== pmp_match_32
Given a physical address, see if any PMP entry matches.

If there is a complete match, return the PmpCfg that guards the region.
If there is no match or a partial match, report that result.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `PmpMatchResult, PmpCfg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH>`
! paddr
! 1
h! `U32`
! access_size
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<12> pmpcfg0_addr = 0x3a0;
Bits<12> pmpaddr0_addr = 0x3b0;
for pass:[(]U32 i = 0; i < NUM_PMP_ENTRIES; i++) {
  Bits<12> pmpcfg_idx = pmpcfg0_addr pass:[+] (i / 4);
  Bits<6> shamt = (i % 4) * 8;
  Csr pmpcfg_csr = xref:#udb-function-direct_csr_lookup[direct_csr_lookup]pass:[(]pmpcfg_idx);
  PmpCfg cfg = (xref:#udb-function-csr_hw_read[csr_hw_read]pass:[(]pmpcfg_csr) >> shamt)[7:0];
  Bits<12> pmpaddr_idx = pmpaddr0_addr pass:[+] i;
  Csr pmpaddr_csr = xref:#udb-function-direct_csr_lookup[direct_csr_lookup]pass:[(]pmpaddr_idx);
  Bits<32> pmpaddr_csr_value = xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_read[csr_sw_read]pass:[(]pmpaddr_csr);
  Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH> range_base = 0;
  Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH> range_limit = 0;
  if pass:[(]cfg.A == $bits(PmpCfg_A::TOR)) {
    if pass:[(]i == 0) {
      range_base = 0;
    } else {
      Csr tor_pmpaddr_csr = xref:#udb-function-direct_csr_lookup[direct_csr_lookup]pass:[(]pmpaddr_idx - 1);
      range_base = xref:#udb-function-csr_sw_read[csr_sw_read]pass:[(]tor_pmpaddr_csr)[PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 1:0];
    }
    range_limit = (pmpaddr_csr_value)[PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 1:0] - 1;
  } else if pass:[(]cfg.A == $bits(PmpCfg_A::NAPOT)) {
    Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 1> pmpaddr_value = pmpaddr_csr_value[PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 3:0];
    Bits<PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 1> mask = pmpaddr_value ^ (pmpaddr_value pass:[+] 1);
    range_base = pmpaddr_value & ~mask;
    range_limit = range_base pass:[+] mask;
  } else if pass:[(]cfg.A == $bits(PmpCfg_A::NA4)) {
    range_base = pmpaddr_csr_value[PHYS_ADDR_WIDTH - 1:0];
    range_limit = range_base pass:[+] 3;
  }
  if pass:[(]((paddr >> 2) >= range_base) && (((paddr pass:[+] (access_size / 8) - 1) >> 2) <= range_limit)) {
    return PmpMatchResult::FullMatch, cfg;
  } else if pass:[(]!(((paddr pass:[+] (access_size / 8) - 1) < range_base) || (paddr >= range_limit))) {
    return PmpMatchResult::PartialMatch, -;
  }
}
return PmpMatchResult::NoMatch, -;
----

[#udb-function-raise]
=== raise
Raise synchronous exception number `exception_code`.

The exception may be imprecise, and will cause execution to enter an
unpredictable state, if PRECISE_SYNCHRONOUS_EXCEPTIONS is false.

Otherwise, the exception will be precise.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `ExceptionCode`
! exception_code
! 1
h! `PrivilegeMode`
! from_mode
! 2
h! `XReg`
! tval
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]!PRECISE_SYNCHRONOUS_EXCEPTIONS) {
  xref:#udb-function-unpredictable[unpredictable]pass:[(]"Imprecise synchronous exception");
} else {
  xref:#udb-function-raise_precise[raise_precise]pass:[(]exception_code, from_mode, tval);
}
----

[#udb-function-raise_precise]
=== raise_precise
Raise synchronous exception number `exception_code`.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `ExceptionCode`
! exception_code
! 1
h! `PrivilegeMode`
! from_mode
! 2
h! `XReg`
! tval
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
PrivilegeMode handling_mode = xref:#udb-function-exception_handling_mode[exception_handling_mode]pass:[(]exception_code);
if pass:[(]handling_mode == PrivilegeMode::M) {
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mepc[mepc]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mepc-PC[PC] = $pc;
  if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-mtval_readonly?[mtval_readonly?]pass:[(])) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mtval[mtval]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mtval-VALUE[VALUE] = xref:#udb-function-mtval_for[mtval_for]pass:[(]exception_code, tval);
  }
  $pc = {CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mtvec[mtvec]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mtvec-BASE[BASE], 2'b00};
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mcause[mcause]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mcause-INT[INT] = 1'b0;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mcause[mcause]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mcause-CODE[CODE] = $bits(exception_code);
  if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::H) && CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-H[H] == 1) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mtval2[mtval2]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mtval2-VALUE[VALUE] = 0;
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mtinst[mtinst]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mtinst-VALUE[VALUE] = 0;
    if pass:[(]from_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU || from_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS) {
      if pass:[(]MXLEN == 32) {
        CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatush[mstatush]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatush-MPV[MPV] = 1;
      } else {
        CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPV[MPV] = 1;
      }
    } else {
      if pass:[(]MXLEN == 32) {
        CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatush[mstatush]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatush-MPV[MPV] = 0;
      } else {
        CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPV[MPV] = 0;
      }
    }
  }
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MPP[MPP] = $bits(from_mode);
} else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1 && (handling_mode == PrivilegeMode::S)) {
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-sepc[sepc]].xref:#udb-csrfield-sepc-PC[PC] = $pc;
  if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-stval_readonly?[stval_readonly?]pass:[(])) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-stval[stval]].xref:#udb-csrfield-stval-VALUE[VALUE] = xref:#udb-function-stval_for[stval_for]pass:[(]exception_code, tval);
  }
  $pc = {CSR[xref:#udb-csr-stvec[stvec]].xref:#udb-csrfield-stvec-BASE[BASE], 2'b00};
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-scause[scause]].xref:#udb-csrfield-scause-INT[INT] = 1'b0;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-scause[scause]].xref:#udb-csrfield-scause-CODE[CODE] = $bits(exception_code);
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SPP[SPP] = $bits(from_mode)[0];
  if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-H[H] == 1) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-htval[htval]].xref:#udb-csrfield-htval-VALUE[VALUE] = 0;
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-htinst[htinst]].xref:#udb-csrfield-htinst-VALUE[VALUE] = 0;
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-SPV[SPV] = $bits(from_mode)[2];
    if pass:[(]from_mode == PrivilegeMode::VU || from_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS) {
      CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-SPV[SPV] = 1;
      if pass:[(]((exception_code == ExceptionCode::Breakpoint) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_BREAKPOINT)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::LoadAddressMisaligned) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_LOAD_MISALIGNED)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAddressMisaligned) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_STORE_AMO_MISALIGNED)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::InstructionAddressMisaligned) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_INSTRUCTION_MISALIGNED)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::LoadAccessFault) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_LOAD_ACCESS_FAULT)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAccessFault) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_STORE_AMO_ACCESS_FAULT)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::InstructionAccessFault) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_INSTRUCTION_ACCESS_FAULT)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::LoadPageFault) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_LOAD_PAGE_FAULT)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::StoreAmoPageFault) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_STORE_AMO_PAGE_FAULT)) || ((exception_code == ExceptionCode::InstructionPageFault) && (REPORT_VA_IN_STVAL_ON_INSTRUCTION_PAGE_FAULT))) {
        CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-GVA[GVA] = 1;
      } else {
        CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-GVA[GVA] = 0;
      }
      CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-SPVP[SPVP] = $bits(from_mode)[0];
    } else {
      CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-SPV[SPV] = 0;
      CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-GVA[GVA] = 0;
    }
  }
} else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-H[H] == 1 && (handling_mode == PrivilegeMode::VS)) {
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsepc[vsepc]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsepc-PC[PC] = $pc;
  if pass:[(]!xref:#udb-function-vstval_readonly?[vstval_readonly?]pass:[(])) {
    CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vstval[vstval]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vstval-VALUE[VALUE] = xref:#udb-function-vstval_for[vstval_for]pass:[(]exception_code, tval);
  }
  $pc = {CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vstvec[vstvec]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vstvec-BASE[BASE], 2'b00};
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vscause[vscause]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vscause-INT[INT] = 1'b0;
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vscause[vscause]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vscause-CODE[CODE] = $bits(exception_code);
  CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-SPP[SPP] = $bits(from_mode)[0];
}
xref:#udb-function-set_mode[set_mode]pass:[(]handling_mode);
xref:#udb-function-abort_current_instruction[abort_current_instruction]pass:[(]);
----

[#udb-function-read_device_32]
=== read_device_32 (builtin)
Read 32 bits from non-memory-mapped device.
Such devices have own addresses not related to memory map.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Bits<32>`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! dev_addr
!===

|===


[#udb-function-read_memory]
=== read_memory
Read from virtual memory.

  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `XReg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `U32`
! LEN
! 1
h! `XReg`
! virtual_address
! 2
h! `Bits<INSTR_ENC_SIZE>`
! encoding
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Boolean aligned = xref:#udb-function-is_naturally_aligned[is_naturally_aligned]pass:[(]LEN, virtual_address);
XReg physical_address;
if pass:[(]aligned) {
  return xref:#udb-function-read_memory_aligned[read_memory_aligned]pass:[(]LEN, virtual_address, encoding, 1'b0, 1'b0);
}
if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_MAX_ATOMICITY_GRANULE_SIZE > 0) {
  xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]MISALIGNED_LDST_EXCEPTION_PRIORITY == "low", "Invalid config: can't mix low-priority misaligned exceptions with large atomicity granule");
  physical_address = (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1) ? xref:#udb-function-translate[translate]pass:[(]virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Read, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), encoding).paddr : virtual_address;
  if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-misaligned_is_atomic?[misaligned_is_atomic?]pass:[(]LEN, physical_address)) {
    xref:#udb-function-access_check[access_check]pass:[(]physical_address, LEN, virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Read, ExceptionCode::LoadAccessFault, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]));
    return xref:#udb-function-read_physical_memory[read_physical_memory]pass:[(]LEN, physical_address);
  }
}
if pass:[(]!MISALIGNED_LDST) {
  if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_LDST_EXCEPTION_PRIORITY == "low") {
    physical_address = (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1) ? xref:#udb-function-translate[translate]pass:[(]virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Read, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), encoding).paddr : virtual_address;
    xref:#udb-function-access_check[access_check]pass:[(]physical_address, LEN, virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Read, ExceptionCode::LoadAccessFault, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]));
  }
  xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::LoadAddressMisaligned, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), virtual_address);
} else {
  if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_SPLIT_STRATEGY == "sequential_bytes") {
    XReg result = 0;
    for pass:[(]U32 I = 0; I < (LEN / 8); I++) {
      result = result | (xref:#udb-function-read_memory_aligned[read_memory_aligned]pass:[(]8, virtual_address pass:[+] I, encoding, 1'b0, 1'b0) pass:[`]<< (8 * I));
    }
    return result;
  } else if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_SPLIT_STRATEGY == "custom") {
    xref:#udb-function-unpredictable[unpredictable]pass:[(]"An implementation is free to break a misaligned access any way, leading to unpredictable behavior when any part of the misaligned access causes an exception");
  }
}
----

[#udb-function-read_memory_aligned]
=== read_memory_aligned
Read from virtual memory using a known aligned address.

If +rl+ is 1, then the load also acts as a memory model release (applied after all
checks pass but before the physical read).
If +aq+ is 1, then the load also acts as a memory model acquire (applied after the read).
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `XReg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `U32`
! LEN
! 1
h! `XReg`
! virtual_address
! 2
h! `Bits<INSTR_ENC_SIZE>`
! encoding
! 3
h! `Bits<1>`
! aq
! 4
h! `Bits<1>`
! rl
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
TranslationResult result;
if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1) {
  result = xref:#udb-function-translate[translate]pass:[(]virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Read, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), encoding);
} else {
  result.paddr = virtual_address;
}
xref:#udb-function-access_check[access_check]pass:[(]result.paddr, LEN, virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Read, ExceptionCode::LoadAccessFault, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]));
if pass:[(]rl == 1'b1) {
  xref:#udb-function-memory_model_release[memory_model_release]pass:[(]);
}
XReg value = xref:#udb-function-read_physical_memory[read_physical_memory]pass:[(]LEN, result.paddr);
if pass:[(]aq == 1'b1) {
  xref:#udb-function-memory_model_acquire[memory_model_acquire]pass:[(]);
}
return value;
----

if pass:[(]len == 8) {
  return xref:#udb-function-read_physical_memory_8[read_physical_memory_8]pass:[(]paddr);
} else if pass:[(]len == 16) {
  return xref:#udb-function-read_physical_memory_16[read_physical_memory_16]pass:[(]paddr);
} else if pass:[(]len == 32) {
  return xref:#udb-function-read_physical_memory_32[read_physical_memory_32]pass:[(]paddr);
} else if pass:[(]len == 64) {
  return xref:#udb-function-read_physical_memory_64[read_physical_memory_64]pass:[(]paddr);
} else {
  xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]false, "Invalid len");
}

[#udb-function-refresh_pending_interrupts]
=== refresh_pending_interrupts
refreshes the calculation of a pending interrupt

needs to be called after any state update that could change a pending interrupt. This includes:
   - CSR[mip]
   - CSR[mie]
   - CSR[mstatus].MIE
   - CSR[mstatus].SIE
   - CSR[vsstatus].SIE
   - CSR[mideleg]
   - CSR[sideleg]
   - CSR[hideleg]
   - CSR[hvip]
   - CSR[hgeip]
   - CSR[hgeie]
   - mode changes
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

None

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Bits<MXLEN> pending_ints = CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mip[CSR[mip]]].sw_read() & $bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mie[CSR[mie]]]);
if pass:[(]pending_ints == 0) {
  pending_and_enabled_interrupts = 0;
  return ;
}
Boolean HAS_MIDELEG = xref:#udb-function-implemented_version?[implemented_version?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::S, "<= 1.9.1") || (xref:#udb-function-implemented_version?[implemented_version?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::S, "> 1.9.1") && xref:#udb-function-implemented_version?[implemented_version?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::Sm, "> 1.9.1"));
Bits<MXLEN> mmode_enabled_ints = ((xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::M) && (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-MIE[MIE] == 1'b0)) ? 0 : ($bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mie[CSR[mie]]]) & (HAS_MIDELEG ? ~$bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mideleg[CSR[mideleg]]]) : ~MXLEN'0));
Bits<MXLEN> mmode_pending_and_enabled = pending_ints & mmode_enabled_ints;
if pass:[(]mmode_pending_and_enabled != 0) {
  pending_and_enabled_interrupts = mmode_pending_and_enabled;
  return ;
}
if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1'b1) {
  Bits<MXLEN> smode_enabled_ints = ((xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::M) || (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SIE[SIE] == 1'b0)) ? 0 : $bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mie[CSR[mie]]]) & ($bits(CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mideleg[CSR[mideleg]]]));
  Bits<MXLEN> smode_pending_and_enabled = pending_ints & smode_enabled_ints;
  if pass:[(]smode_pending_and_enabled != 0) {
    pending_and_enabled_interrupts = smode_pending_and_enabled;
    return ;
  }
}
pending_and_enabled_interrupts = 0;
----

[#udb-function-set_mode]

  xref:#udb-function-notify_mode_change[notify_mode_change]pass:[(]new_mode, current_mode);
  current_mode = new_mode;
  xref:#udb-function-refresh_pending_interrupts[refresh_pending_interrupts]pass:[(]);

[#udb-function-sext]
=== sext
Sign extend `value` starting at `first_extended_bit`.

Bits [`XLEN-1`:`first_extended_bit`] of the return value
should get the value of bit (`first_extended bit - 1`).
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `XReg`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! value
! 1
h! `XReg`
! first_extended_bit
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]first_extended_bit == MXLEN) {
  return value;
} else {
  Bits<1> sign = value[first_extended_bit - 1];
  for pass:[(]U32 i = MXLEN - 1; i >= first_extended_bit; i--) {
    value[i] = sign;
  }
  return value;
}
----

[#udb-function-sync_read_after_write_device]
=== sync_read_after_write_device (builtin)
Synchronize non-memory-mapped device read-after-write.
Such devices have own addresses not related to memory map.
Devices specified by device bitmask (up to 5 devices).
Stalls processor till condtions met.
Conditions are that last device output started or completed (depends on argument).
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `Boolean`
! completed
! 1
h! `Bits<5>`
! device_bitmask
!===

|===

Such devices have own addresses not related to memory map.
Devices specified by device bitmask (up to 5 devices).
Stalls processor till condtions met.
Conditions are that last device input started or completed (depends on argument).
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
