[#udb-function-translate]
=== translate
Translate a virtual address for operation type +op+ that appears to execute at
+effective_mode+.

The translation will depend on the effective privilege mode.

May raise a Page Fault or Access Fault.

The final physical address is *not* access checked (for PMP, PMA, etc., violations).
(though intermediate page table reads will be)
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `TranslationResult`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! vaddr
! 1
h! `MemoryOperation`
! op
! 2
h! `PrivilegeMode`
! effective_mode
! 3
h! `Bits<INSTR_ENC_SIZE>`
! encoding
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Boolean cached_translation_valid;
CachedTranslationResult cached_translation_result;
cached_translation_result = xref:#udb-function-cached_translation[cached_translation]pass:[(]vaddr, op);
if pass:[(]cached_translation_result.valid) {
  return cached_translation_result.result;
}
TranslationResult result;
if pass:[(]effective_mode == PrivilegeMode::M) {
  result.paddr = vaddr;
  return result;
}
SatpMode translation_mode = xref:#udb-function-current_translation_mode[current_translation_mode]pass:[(]effective_mode);
if pass:[(]translation_mode == SatpMode::Reserved) {
  if pass:[(]op == MemoryOperation::Read) {
    xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::LoadPageFault, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), vaddr);
  } else if pass:[(]op == MemoryOperation::Write || op == MemoryOperation::ReadModifyWrite) {
    xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::StoreAmoPageFault, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), vaddr);
  } else {
    xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]op == MemoryOperation::Fetch, "Unexpected memory operation");
    xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::InstructionPageFault, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), vaddr);
  }
}
if pass:[(]translation_mode == SatpMode::Bare) {
  result.paddr = vaddr;
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) == 32 && translation_mode == SatpMode::Sv32) {
  result = xref:#udb-function-stage1_page_walk[stage1_page_walk]pass:[(]32, 34, 32, 2, vaddr, op, effective_mode, encoding);
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) == 64 && translation_mode == SatpMode::Sv39) {
  result = xref:#udb-function-stage1_page_walk[stage1_page_walk]pass:[(]39, 56, 64, 3, vaddr, op, effective_mode, encoding);
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) == 64 && translation_mode == SatpMode::Sv48) {
  result = xref:#udb-function-stage1_page_walk[stage1_page_walk]pass:[(]48, 56, 64, 4, vaddr, op, effective_mode, encoding);
} else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-xlen[xlen]pass:[(]) == 64 && translation_mode == SatpMode::Sv57) {
  result = xref:#udb-function-stage1_page_walk[stage1_page_walk]pass:[(]57, 56, 64, 5, vaddr, op, effective_mode, encoding);
} else {
  xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]false, "Unexpected SatpMode");
}
xref:#udb-function-maybe_cache_translation[maybe_cache_translation]pass:[(]vaddr, op, result);
return result;
----

[#udb-function-write_memory]
=== write_memory
Write to virtual memory
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `U32`
! LEN
! 1
h! `XReg`
! virtual_address
! 2
h! `XReg`
! value
! 3
h! `Bits<INSTR_ENC_SIZE>`
! encoding
!===

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
Boolean aligned = xref:#udb-function-is_naturally_aligned[is_naturally_aligned]pass:[(]LEN, virtual_address);
XReg physical_address;
if pass:[(]aligned) {
  xref:#udb-function-write_memory_aligned[write_memory_aligned]pass:[(]LEN, virtual_address, value, encoding, 1'b0, 1'b0);
  return ;
}
if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_MAX_ATOMICITY_GRANULE_SIZE > 0) {
  xref:#udb-function-assert[assert]pass:[(]MISALIGNED_LDST_EXCEPTION_PRIORITY == "low", "Invalid config: can't mix low-priority misaligned exceptions with large atomicity granule");
  physical_address = (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1) ? xref:#udb-function-translate[translate]pass:[(]virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Write, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), encoding).paddr : virtual_address;
  if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-misaligned_is_atomic?[misaligned_is_atomic?]pass:[(]LEN, physical_address)) {
    xref:#udb-function-access_check[access_check]pass:[(]physical_address, LEN, virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Write, ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAccessFault, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]));
    xref:#udb-function-write_physical_memory[write_physical_memory]pass:[(]LEN, physical_address, value);
    return ;
  }
}
if pass:[(]!MISALIGNED_LDST) {
  if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_LDST_EXCEPTION_PRIORITY == "low") {
    physical_address = (CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-S[S] == 1) ? xref:#udb-function-translate[translate]pass:[(]virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Write, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]), encoding).paddr : virtual_address;
    xref:#udb-function-access_check[access_check]pass:[(]physical_address, LEN, virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Write, ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAccessFault, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]));
  }
  xref:#udb-function-raise[raise]pass:[(]ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAddressMisaligned, xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]), virtual_address);
} else {
  if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_SPLIT_STRATEGY == "sequential_bytes") {
    for pass:[(]U32 I = 0; I < (LEN / 8); I++) {
      xref:#udb-function-write_memory_aligned[write_memory_aligned]pass:[(]8, virtual_address pass:[+] I, (value >> (8 * I))[7:0], encoding, 1'b0, 1'b0);
    }
  } else if pass:[(]MISALIGNED_SPLIT_STRATEGY == "custom") {
    xref:#udb-function-unpredictable[unpredictable]pass:[(]"An implementation is free to break a misaligned access any way, leading to unpredictable behavior when any part of the misaligned access causes an exception");
  }
}
----

[#udb-function-write_memory_aligned]
=== write_memory_aligned
Write to virtual memory using a known aligned address.

If +rl+ is 1, then the store also acts as a memory model release (applied after all
checks pass but before the physical write).
If +aq+ is 1, then the store also acts as a memory model acquire.
  

[cols="1,4"]

! 4
h! `Bits<1>`

! 5
h! `Bits<1>`
! rl

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]

xref:#udb-function-access_check[access_check]pass:[(]physical_address, LEN, virtual_address, MemoryOperation::Write, ExceptionCode::StoreAmoAccessFault, xref:#udb-function-effective_ldst_mode[effective_ldst_mode]pass:[(]));

  xref:#udb-function-memory_model_release[memory_model_release]pass:[(]);

[#udb-function-write_physical_memory_32]

|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! paddr
! 1
h! `Bits<32>`
! value
!===

|===


[#udb-function-write_physical_memory_8]
=== write_physical_memory_8 (builtin)
Write a byte to physical memory.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `void`
h| Arguments
a|

[cols="1,4,4"]
!===
! Idx ! Type ! Name

! 0
h! `XReg`
! paddr
! 1
h! `Bits<8>`
! value
!===

[#udb-function-xlen]
=== xlen
Returns the effective XLEN for the current privilege mode.
  

[cols="1,4"]
|===
h| Return Type h| `Bits<8>`
h| Arguments
a|

None

|===

[source,idl,subs="specialchars,macros"]
----
if pass:[(]MXLEN == 32) {
  return 32;
} else {
  if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::M) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-MXL[MXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
      return 32;
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-misa[misa]].xref:#udb-csrfield-misa-MXL[MXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return 64;
    } else {
      xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
    }
  } else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::S) && xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::S) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SXL[SXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
      return 32;
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-SXL[SXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return 64;
    } else {
      xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
    }
  } else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::U) && xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::U) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-UXL[UXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
      return 32;
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-mstatus[mstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-mstatus-UXL[UXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return 64;
    } else {
      xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
    }
  } else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::H) && xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::VS) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-VSXL[VSXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
      return 32;
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-hstatus[hstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-hstatus-VSXL[VSXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return 64;
    } else {
      xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
    }
  } else if pass:[(]xref:#udb-function-implemented?[implemented?]pass:[(]ExtensionName::H) && xref:#udb-function-mode[mode]pass:[(]) == PrivilegeMode::VU) {
    if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-UXL[UXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN32)) {
      return 32;
    } else if pass:[(]CSR[xref:#udb-csr-vsstatus[vsstatus]].xref:#udb-csrfield-vsstatus-UXL[UXL] == $bits(XRegWidth::XLEN64)) {
      return 64;
    } else {
      xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
    }
  } else {
    xref:#udb-function-unreachable[unreachable]pass:[(]);
  }
}
----
